Current Commentary

On Anglo-French Talks and Coordination - Heng 46

That the Anglo-French talks would quickly succeed was anticipated by commentators long ago. This is because, first, the British desire for peace in Europe is no different from the French. Second, the enemy in the British mind is Germany, not France. Baldwin's statement that Britain's frontier is on the Rhine reveals his intentions. Third, after the Saar issue was resolved, Britain's Eden hoped that all countries would take further action to lay the foundation for the European situation. As for the French side, it also considers alliance with Britain a necessary condition. If Britain cooperates with France, then concerns on the Western European side can be completely dispelled. Therefore, regardless of how successful French diplomacy is and how many countries are allied, alliance with Britain is still the key to controlling Germany. Given these points, the coordination between Britain and France is a natural result and not surprising.

Looking at the results of the current Anglo-French talks based on foreign dispatches, there are three main points: 1. Establishing a "Sky Pact"; 2. Addressing the Central European issue, with Britain agreeing to the Rome Accords; 3. Addressing disarmament issues in accordance with the Five-Power Declaration of 1932. The "Sky Pact" is to compensate for the shortcomings of the Locarno Pact and ensure peace in Western Europe. In recent days, air warfare has been developing rapidly. Britain and Germany are separated only by a narrow strip of water and are vulnerable to attacks. France and Germany are even more at risk due to their close proximity. This Anglo-French plan is no less than a disguised form of air force cooperation. The Central European Pact, based on the Rome Accords, aims not only to guarantee the independence of Austria but also to maintain the status quo in Central Europe. Britain's agreement on this will turn the precarious situation in Central Europe from danger to safety. The disarmament issue, in accordance with the Five-Power Declaration, means seeking equality in armaments without jeopardizing the security of each country. It also means that if Germany wants to increase its armaments, it must do so on the condition of joining the above two pacts and returning to the League of Nations. Therefore, future issues on the European diplomatic stage will inevitably focus on these points. Furthermore, if the Five-Power Declaration is used as a basis for discussion, then Austria, Hungary, etc., also have the right to rearm. In this way, although peace in Europe will be strengthened due to the conclusion of various pacts, the quantity of armaments will greatly increase.

Since the Anglo-French talks have yielded such results, the problem from now on lies with Germany. According to yesterday's European dispatches, Germany is quite satisfied with the results of the Anglo-French talks and has also expressed a willingness to discuss the Central European Pact. From this, it seems that Germany has abandoned its former concept of relying solely on military force and is seeking international coordination. If there are no changes along the way, Germany's return to the League of Nations is within expectations. However, there are still many conflicts between Germany and France, and full coordination may require a long period of negotiations and compromises.

Over the past year, Europe has been fraught with danger, with ominous clouds gathering and numerous tragedies occurring, far exceeding those on the eve of the Great War. The amount of ammunition stockpiles is also no less than in those years. Therefore, those who care about current events are all alarmed, believing that a second world war is about to break out. Unexpectedly, the crises have repeatedly been averted, and by today, the European situation has largely stabilized. The contradictions and conflicts between European countries have also decreased. The most notable examples are the improvement of relations between France and the Little Entente with Russia, the elimination of the Franco-Italian conflict, and the reconstruction of Anglo-French coordination. Therefore, although the past year has been the most dangerous time for Europe, in reality, it has been a period of transformation from danger to safety in the European situation.

Japanese Government Considers Reinstating Anglo-Japanese Alliance 51

Closing of the International Labour Bureau Governing Body Meeting 52

(Geneva) The 69th session of the administrative body of the International Labour Bureau began on January 29th and closed on February 2nd. My representative, Li Pingheng, was absent, and Bao Huaguo represented. In an important closed-door meeting held today, after the discussion, a Central News Agency reporter was told that the agenda of this session was extremely heavy, with a total of 18 proposals. Among them, two were particularly important in relation to China. One was the issue of the eight seats for the world's major industrial countries. After the United States and the Soviet Union joined the International Labour Organization, they should be given important permanent seats in the administrative bodies. Therefore, the International Labour Organization has re-selected the eight major industrial countries. The selection criteria used this time are: (1) the total number of people actually residing; (2) imports and exports; (3) the annual dues borne to the League of Nations; (4) industrial activity. It is found that the above four listed standards are more favorable to China than those set in 1922. However, there are a total of 62 member states of the International Labour Organization, and experts have compared only 20 for selection. The Chinese representative in the meeting advocated supporting the selection criteria but did not agree with the comparison method adopted. After fierce debate, the proposals put forward by the Chinese and other government representatives were finally passed. The second was the selection of the agenda for next year's general meeting. Because next year's agenda is too heavy, a part of the proposals must be removed. Among them, the proposal submitted by the Chinese representative in 1933 regarding the seeking and placement of immigrant workers was also under discussion as to whether it should be removed. The Chinese representative and representatives of some governments and workers all advocated including it in the agenda, but the employer representatives and most government representatives were afraid of insufficient time and advocated making it a backup. It has been passed by the meeting, it is said. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 5th)

Our Country's League of Nations Membership Dues 53

Annual payment of forty-two units starting this year

All arrears from the previous four years are completely waived

Past arrears are amortized over thirty years

(Geneva) The Chinese government, due to financial and economic difficulties and frequent disasters over the years, specifically requested the League of Nations to reduce its membership dues and waive the accumulated arrears year by year. This request was reviewed by the Fourth Committee of the League of Nations General Assembly last year and handed over to the Secretariat of the League of Nations for handling. Now, the League of Nations Expenditure Allocation Committee and the Special Committee for Organizing Arrears of Membership Dues, established by the Secretariat, unanimously resolved that from 1935 until a new chapter is drafted for the membership dues, China will pay 42 units of membership dues each year, with each unit amounting to 30,294 gold francs and 65 centimes. As for the arrears from 1931 to 1934, they will be exempted. The old arrears from previous years before 1930, which were organized by the agreement established in 1930, will be paid off in 30 years starting from 1935, it is said. Sixth Havas dispatch)

Japanese Troops Stationed in Eastern Provinces 54

According to the Treaty of Portsmouth

Soviet Russia has the right to protest

(Moscow) According to a Japanese news agency, the Japanese authorities believe that the Soviet Union has no right to raise the issue of the strength of the Japanese garrison in Manchuria. Izvestia commented on this, saying, "The Soviet Union's automatic abolition of the rights conferred upon it by the Treaty of Portsmouth has not deprived that constraint of its power to bind Japan. Tokyo seems too vague about this obvious truth. It should be known that the Soviet Union cannot grant Japan any new rights, and at the same time, it will never allow Japan to relax its obligations under the Treaty of Portsmouth (further confirmed by the Sino-Soviet Beijing Agreement of January 2, 1925). The fact that the Soviet government is unwilling to station troops on the Chinese Eastern Railway does not give Japan any right to station troops in Manchuria several times larger than allowed by the Treaty of Portsmouth," it said. (TASS dispatch on the 5th)

Japanese Naval Minister Clarifies Naval Stance 55

Implement independent armament after the naval conference breaks down

Does not hesitate to compete with the United States in building ships and increasing defenses

(Tokyo) At the fourth subcommittee meeting of the budget this afternoon, Naval Minister Osumi explained the attitude of the Japanese Navy in response to questions from various members. The summary of his responses is as follows: In the initial naval reduction negotiations, Japanese representative Vice Admiral Yamamoto presented the figures of the tonnage held by various countries to the British representative in a private meeting, but this was Vice Admiral Yamamoto's private proposal and did not show the actual tonnage that Japan wanted to build. However, if the naval reduction conference breaks down, we originally wanted to establish an independent armament plan, but it has not yet been started. Also, regarding the Pacific defense issue, if the United States builds air and naval bases in the Aleutian Islands, Japan will expand its armaments in Taiwan and other places. The United States is now starting to build battleships, and Japan is scheduled to retrofit battleships and aircraft carriers next year (from April this year to March next year), and retrofit some auxiliary ships the following year, it is said. United States Convenes World Cotton Conference 58

(Washington) The United States will soon hold a World Cotton Conference in Washington. It invited Brazil to send a delegation to participate last week, and now it has informally invited Britain to invite India and British Sudan to send representatives to the meeting. Senators from the cotton-producing states in the southern United States advocate finding ways to remedy the situation of the American cotton industry and insist that the government choose one of the following two methods: (1) Require other cotton-producing countries that compete with the United States to reduce production; (2) Or abolish the measures to reduce domestic production. Most senators even demand that the American cotton industry implement a dumping policy to make other cotton-producing countries submit. In 1933, the combined cotton planting area of Brazil, India, and Egypt was 10,100,000 hectares, while last year it was 11,300,000 hectares. In the past six years, the average number of cotton bales sold by India each year was 2 million, Egypt sold 1.5 million, and Brazil sold 273,000, it is said. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

British and French Jointly Suggest German Government to Study Carefully 61

Göring Will Be Ordered to Visit London

Discussing the Sky Pact Plan

The Modalities of Establishing Regional Pacts Await Questioning

(London) The agreement reached between Britain and France this time is of great help to European peace. Today, the French and German governments are paying attention to this move. German leader Hitler, Foreign Minister Neurath, and other important officials held an emergency political meeting to discuss this matter for a long time. After the meeting, no official announcement was issued. Roughly, Germany's second step will be to have the German ambassadors to London and Paris raise some questions regarding the actual meaning of certain items in the London proposals. Hitler had originally scheduled to meet with Archbishop Mueller today, but the meeting was temporarily postponed due to the convening of the emergency political meeting. The atmosphere in Paris discussing this agreement is completely different from that in Berlin. Premier Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval were sincerely congratulated by cabinet members. President Lebrun also praised them greatly, saying that the London talks had achieved gratifying results. Flandin explained the London proposals in the Chamber of Deputies today, saying that the agreement between the two sides would never interfere with the League of Nations' efforts to establish a universal disarmament treaty. The agreement between Britain and France, in short, is to deal with issues concerning Germany's rearmament, and involves the maintenance of Austria's independence and territorial integrity, the Sky Defense Pact, and Germany's return to the League of Nations, it is said. (Reuters dispatch on the 5th)

(London) According to the report of Sir Phipps, the ambassador to Germany received by the government, Germany will be able to submit a response to the joint proposal of Britain and France to the countries concerned after half a month. (Havas dispatch on the 5th) (Berlin) The Berlin correspondent of the Daily Mail now believes that if British Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden do not come to Berlin, then Prussian Governor General Göring will go to London in his capacity as Minister of Aviation to discuss with the British government the plan to conclude a Sky Defense Pact contained in the recent British-French agreement. This matter is currently under consideration by the Berlin government. (It is said that Simon and Eden's visit to Germany has been denied by British officials.)

(Havas dispatch on the 6th)

(Berlin) The cabinet held a small group meeting, chaired by Hitler, to study the declaration issued by Britain and France after the end of the London talks, in order to determine the meaning of the various possible ways contained therein. German political figures seem to have an attitude that is not as optimistic today as it was yesterday, but they all admit that before Britain and France issued the declaration, the ambassadors of the two countries to Germany informed Berlin of its contents, which shows that the two countries did not want to create a fait accompli first and then ask Germany to recognize it. In general, it is believed that the spirit of cooperation expressed in the London declaration, if it is to be translated into reality, must be negotiated, but in order to determine the outline of this negotiation, it is necessary to hold long-term negotiations in the diplomatic field. German figures have raised some objections to the proposal to conclude a Sky Pact, saying that Britain and France are asking Germany to sign a Sky Pact, which assumes that Germany has an air force. However, it should be known that "Germany is bound by the Treaty of Versailles and does not have an air force." In addition, the question of regional pacts (Danube Pact and Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact), what status will they have within the scope of the future general agreement, and the right to equal armament, which is only proposed in principle without concrete explanation, in what form will it be realized within the scope of the general disarmament treaty in the future, are all questions that Germany wants to hear in detail. Therefore, regarding the various methods mentioned in the British-French statement, the German government will soon raise questions to Britain and France. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

French Chamber of Deputies Listens to the Course of the London Negotiations 62

Premier Explains the Importance of the Air Defense Pact

(Paris) This afternoon, the Chamber of Deputies discussed the results of the recent British-French talks. Premier Flandin replied to the question of Socialist member Léon Blum and issued a declaration, saying that France has no intention of abandoning the League of Nations on various international issues. The purpose of the London talks is only to consolidate European peace and to express the complete common opinion of the two governments on peace organizations. Although an international security organization is not available without an international defense organization, air raids are the most worrisome for security. Therefore, Britain and France both agree to conclude a regional pact to provide mutual assistance in the air when necessary. The French side advocates expanding the scope of this Sky Pact, and all Western European countries that are willing to have peace should join this pact to jointly avoid the danger of the sky. However, after the British and French governments decided to invite Germany, Italy, and Belgium to hold negotiations first, it was because these three countries and Britain and France are the signatories of the Locarno Treaty. If they are asked to sign the pact, it is not to increase new constraints, but only to make the actions stipulated in the Locarno Treaty more resolute and faster to implement. Moreover, this kind of action is not punishment, but a warning. When a dispute occurs, once the countries with air forces express cooperation to jointly defend peace, the dispute can be resolved through negotiation without hostile actions occurring. Flandin continued, saying that the British and French governments will hold consultations again after receiving replies from the countries concerned. In short, we deeply hope to build a new dike that is more effective than the old one, so that all attempts to endanger peace will fail. This is the gist of the British-French talks this time, it is said. After Flandin's speech, there was a big applause in the whole place, and the discussion ended. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

Britain Seeks US Opinion on Abolishing Military Clauses of the Treaty 63

(Washington) Regarding the point in the British-French agreement that advocates abolishing Part V of the Treaty of Versailles (i.e., the military clauses), it is now heard that the British government has inquired of US Ambassador Bingham about the attitude of the US government. However, according to the State Department, it has not yet received any official report from Bingham, it is said. According to the post-European War, the United States and Germany separately concluded a peace treaty, and included all the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles. Now, if this clause in the Treaty of Versailles is to be changed, then the consent of the United States should be indirectly sought by Britain and France. Generally speaking, this move is to promote the conclusion of a disarmament treaty, so there will be no difficulties on the part of the US government. However, this matter cannot be discussed until the Berlin government replies, it is said. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

Britain Abandons Traditional Policy, France's Diplomatic Victory 64

Observations of New Yorkers

(New York) According to those familiar with diplomatic situations here, the most important feature of the British-French coordination is the Air Defense Mutual Assistance Pact. This Air Defense Pact indicates that Britain has gradually become suspicious of the increasing German aviation power. It is deeply believed here that Britain has had to effectively abandon its policy of avoiding involvement in continental disputes. Observers believe that since the European War, Britain has always refused to guarantee France to give it assistance in wartime, and France has been demanding this guarantee for fifteen years. By this point, Britain began to grant the guarantee because of the increasing danger of Germany, it is said. (National News Agency dispatch on the 5th)

Excerpts from the Opinions of Various Countries' Public Opinion, German Newspaper 65

It said that the demilitarized zone is not important in military terms, but it concerns German sovereignty and cannot be left unchanged for a long time. Germany respects its national honor and "cannot tolerate being forced into an unequal position because of defeat," it is said. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

Italian Newspaper 66

(Rome) Italian newspapers continue to comment on the results of the British-French London talks. The Italian Daily newspaper said, "The results of the London talks have made the Rome Agreement between Italy and France even stronger. Italian-French cooperation has expanded to become Italian-French-British cooperation. Italy now hopes that Germany will participate directly, so that the scope of cooperation can be expanded to four countries." The newspaper mentioned the issue of the military clauses in Part V of the Treaty of Versailles, saying that Italy supports the movement to amend the treaty, but rejects those who seek to amend the treaty through unilateral actions. If the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles are abolished, then Austria and Hungary also have equal rights, which cannot be denied. This is also the main point of cooperation among the Danube countries, it is said. The "Stampa" newspaper commented on the plan for the Sky Pact, saying that its nature is more progressive than the Locarno Pact. "Il Popolo d'Italia" warned Germany, saying that the various agreements in London and Rome will not be overturned even without Germany's participation, which is what Germany should understand, it is said. (Havas dispatch on the 5th)

Russian Newspaper 67

(Moscow) Izvestia commented on the British-French agreement, saying, "First, the London agreement does not stipulate that Germany's return to the League of Nations can reopen talks on the legalization of German armaments. On the contrary, London has decided that Germany has no right to unilaterally cancel the armament clauses of the Treaty of Versailles. The London compromise decision allows this decision to be changed, but its provisions cannot be considered accurate, because it does not mention the negotiation procedure, and does not stipulate the exact obligation to conclude an Eastern Regional Pact in accordance with the method proposed by the Soviet Union. The French press, which received news from the French delegation, said that these decisions were sufficient to prove that if Germany refused to join the Eastern Regional Pact, then German armaments could not be legalized. If this interpretation of the London compromise proposal is correct, then this compromise can indeed strengthen the position of France and all friends of peace. The London agreement also proposed to conclude a Western Regional Pact, including France, Britain, Belgium, Italy, and Germany. However, it is not appropriate to regard this as a "Aviation Locarno Pact," because in the Locarno Treaty, Italy, Belgium, and Britain are responsible for helping France if Germany attacks France, and helping Germany if France attacks Germany. This pact includes all war preparations, so there is no need to make a special agreement on air strikes. However, according to the new London proposal, if France, Britain, and Belgium encounter a conflict between Italy and Germany over the issue of Austria, and Italy suffers an air strike by Germany, then they must assist Italy. Similarly, if France encounters an air strike by Germany in Britain, then they must assist Britain. This is the new case of the so-called Western Regional Pact. This proposal can be said to be a loss for France, because the Locarno Treaty has already stipulated that if Germany attacks France, then Britain and Italy must come to France's aid. The new addition to this pact is that France must assist the former when Britain and Italy are in conflict with Germany. This proposal is a major new political event, and we should pay attention to whether Germany will also use the weapons it has been accustomed to using in opposing the Eastern Regional Pact. If we pay attention to the German press's reaction to this case, it will be very meaningful. They will surely be mesmerized by the singing in the Four Powers Pact theater, but in general, the London agreement has clearly told Germany that its armament rationalization cannot succeed without agreeing to the work of consolidating peace in Eastern, Western, and Southern Europe. "As for the Soviet Union, it must observe the results of the London negotiations with the greatest calmness. Soviet diplomacy, on the one hand, is based on the protocol signed with France on December 5, and on the other hand, is based on the support of the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente, and must continue to strive for peace. We firmly believe that peace is indivisible. If there is no peace in the East, then the traces of peace will not be in the West," it is said. (TASS dispatch on the 5th)

Mexico City. The British Mexican Eagle Oil Company was originally granted land transfer rights by the government so that it could use it freely. Order 83

On the 6th, the National Government ordered the dismissal of Tang Baoshu, Director-General of the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau, at his request. This order also appointed Shen Shuyu as Director-General of the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau. This order.

Implementation of Parcel and Remittance Exchange Between Inside and Outside the Pass 84

A fee of four jiao is charged per parcel outside the pass.

The maximum amount for drafts is one thousand yuan.

Tianjin Communication: Postal communication between inside and outside the pass has been open for more than two weeks. During these two weeks, apart from the Shanhaiguan Transfer Bureau, which experienced a bombing on the 16th of last month at 6:30 PM, the operations of the responsible handling agencies have been relatively smooth. On average, more than 30,000 items are sent daily from the Tianjin post office to Shanhaiguan for transfer, and more than 5,000 items are transferred via Gubeikou. Among them, Western newspapers average around 2,000 items per day, and postal items from the Northeast reaching foreign countries in Europe and Asia consistently number around 300. When postal communication was initially opened, the Hebei Postal Administration issued a notice stating that items with false organizations or place names written on the envelope would be refused delivery and returned to the original sender. If they could not be returned, the county bureau would hold them for collection. Chinese senders were able to comply and actively avoided writing false organization or place names. Western senders, if it was unavoidable, often wrote "Manchuria" instead. Only the Japanese and Koreans, in an attempt to force us to practically acknowledge the puppet organization, deliberately submitted letters with the titles of false organizations or false place names and, fearing that we would refuse delivery, prominently printed in Japanese newspapers that our post office was deliberately delaying and obstructing communication for foreigners. To clarify the truth, the Hebei Postal Administration issued a notice refuting the false accusations. Previously, the Japanese Kwantung Army, because our post office refused to accept letters with the titles of false organizations, had protested to us through Iga Seiya, the chief of the Shanhaiguan Special Affairs Agency. After Yin Tong and Tao Shangming discussed remedial measures with Iga, it was decided that after postal items destined for outside the pass arrived at the Huitong Transfer Bureau, they would be handed over to the puppet South Suizhong Post Office. When they were transferred from the Gubeikou Huitong Transfer Branch to the puppet South Luanping Post Office, the place names on the mailbags could be altered, and the names of the puppet organizations could be written separately. Iga then went to Changchun to report this matter. It is not yet known whether the Japanese Kwantung Army is satisfied with this arrangement. As for remittances and parcels, the Hebei postal area had prepared everything properly and implemented them on February 1st. The parcel postage fee is slightly higher than before the suspension of postal service, with a fee of four jiao charged for each item sent from outside the pass to Yukou as the final destination, with additional fees for overweight items. Items sent from Yugu to our interior are charged according to our postal rates. Settlements are made every three months, with the Huitong Transfer Bureau responsible. According to Cao Jianting, the head of the Hebei postal service, "After the implementation of remittances and parcels, the expected boom will be in February and early March. However, as the names of the puppet post offices for parcels and remittances are all different from before, it is no longer possible to strictly adhere to the policy of not using puppet organization or agency names. After the opening of postal communication, postal items from outside the pass are handled poorly by the puppet organization and delivered very slowly. Therefore, the section outside the pass is more delayed than postal items within the pass. Those who do not know the truth believe that there is a backlog within the pass, which is not the case." In the Shanhaiguan Huitong Transfer Bureau bombing case, on the 18th of last month, the Shanhaiguan Public Security Bureau arrested eleven suspects, but there was no conclusive confession. On the 27th, a student named Zhang was arrested in Qinhuangdao, admitting that out of patriotic jealousy and hatred, he had contacted his comrades to throw the bomb. There are still two others, one hiding in Ping and one hiding in Qinhuangdao. The Public Security Bureau has dispatched personnel to arrest them separately.

General Accounting Period, Guangzhou's Market is Depressed 85

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce petitions the Provincial Government for Relief

Guangzhou Communication: The market's depression recently is unprecedented in recent years. In previous years, several days before the lunar New Year's Eve, business accounts were busy settling, and all goods sold well. This year, it is the opposite. Many stores in the city have closed down, and the purchasing power of the people has been greatly reduced. In previous years, at the end of the year, the flower markets on Jianglan Street in the west of the city, Shiqipu, and Shuangmendiqnei in the city, with their campanula flowers, narcissus flowers, chrysanthemums, and plum blossoms, bloomed brilliantly and lined the roads, making it dazzling. Citizens chose the best ones to buy, displayed them for events, and adorned the peace. This year, the situation has changed. The above-mentioned locations have sparse floral arrangements, and there is no longer the grand scene of previous years. During this accounting period for merchants, hardly one in a hundred can overcome the difficulties. Therefore, they are mutually implicated and running around to arrange things, but there is no solution. The Economic Committee of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce held a meeting yesterday to discuss measures to relieve the market. The chairman declared on the spot that in this urgent and declining year, the city's finances are depleted, the money market is extremely tight, and several merchants go bankrupt every day due to insufficient turnover. If relief is not urgently sought, the future of Guangzhou's business community will be unimaginable. It was decided to submit a presentation to the government, requesting that the provincial and municipal banks accept commercial warehouse receipts as much as possible so that merchants can turn over cash. At the same time, the government is requested to postpone the collection of merchant debts. As for the settlement of accounts for each store, if the debtor is indeed unable to pay due to business difficulties, accommodation should be provided. In the event of a dispute, the government is also requested to instruct the public security bureaus and branches to properly mediate in order to stabilize commerce and maintain the overall situation. Finally, it was resolved that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce would present to the Provincial Government and the Finance Department, requesting permission to handle the matter in accordance with the above-mentioned situation, and the presentation was drafted and submitted immediately. The original text is as follows: "Presenting for the purpose of petitioning. This Chamber has approved the second meeting record of the Economic Design Committee, which states that Committee Member He Shaohai proposed, 'Now that the Lunar New Year is approaching, the city's commercial financial turnover is difficult. How should it be relieved? Please make a public decision on the case.' It was resolved: (1) Please instruct the provincial and municipal banks to accept commercial warehouse receipts as much as possible to facilitate circulation. (2) The government should postpone the execution of all debt collections from merchants for one month after the Lunar New Year to relieve commercial difficulties, etc. Please forward the matter to the authorities for handling. In view of the fact that commercial transactions are settled at the end of the lunar year, and at this time, the economy is depleted and turnover is difficult, and those who urge the collection of debts are coming one after another, making it impossible to cope, bankruptcies and escapes are more common than usual. Regarding the method of relieving finances, this Chamber has already issued commercial warehouse receipts, and recently the payment of security deposits for use has been waived. Many merchants and people are happy to accept them. If the provincial and municipal banks are accommodated in accepting them, circulation will be easier. As for the current state of the city's finances, it is urgent to maintain it. It seems that the public debts of various merchants should be postponed in order to relieve commercial difficulties, which is also in line with the spirit of cooperation between officials and people. It is reasonable to present this petition to your government and department for examination. We respectfully request that you approve it as requested and order the provincial and municipal banks and all subordinate agencies to comply, in order to provide relief. We will await your instructions and comply. It is for the public good." (January 31)

Serious Rice Famine in Huizhou Prefecture, Southern Anhui 86

Harvests Sharply Reduced, Source Cut Off

Huizhou Communication: The counties of Huizhou Prefecture in southern Anhui are located in remote mountainous areas with little arable land. Local grain production has never been sufficient to feed the people, and most of it has relied on Wuhu, Taiping, Yicheng, Jingde, Raozhou, and other ports. Last year, rice fields in various counties suffered from a widespread drought, and the harvests were sharply reduced. In addition, there was a limited surplus of grain in neighboring areas, or even a ban on exports, cutting off the source, resulting in the current rice famine. Although the special commissioner's office and local authorities in various counties have sent numerous telegrams to the provincial authorities and Shanghai, and Chinese and foreign gentry and merchants have jointly raised funds for relief, the cost of purchasing and transporting grain is considerable. With little porridge and many monks, poor and hungry people are still difficult to benefit from it. The future famine is becoming increasingly serious. The famine situation in each county is explored and recorded as follows:

Qimen: This month, Qimen County is experiencing a complete panic in public food supplies due to the cut-off of grain sources from Jingdezhen River and Jiangxi. Rice prices have soared to five or six sheng per yuan, and there is nowhere to buy it. Flour prices have also soared and there is a shortage in the market. Most of the poor people cook only once every two or three days, half eating sugar powder and vegetables to fill their stomachs. Although the local authorities have distributed 1,000 dan of disaster relief grain, they have not yet sent staff to receive the distribution, and the cries of pain are everywhere. Hoping for the distribution and a quick relief, they are eagerly awaiting food and are extremely keen.

Yi County: Yi County suffered a catastrophic drought last year, and the autumn harvest was very small. The county's grain production is not enough to maintain the supply for one month. The county relies solely on grain transportation from Taiping and other counties for assistance. Recently, due to bandit troubles that have just been quelled, grain merchants from Taiping have not entered the county for a long time. The rice in the city and rural rice shops that should be on sale has been bought and supplied as military food due to the passage of soldiers. As a result, there is no rice on the market in the city recently, and the price of rice has soared to more than 14 yuan per stone. Ordinary poor households have nowhere to buy rice every day and can only fill their stomachs with flour, sweet potatoes, and other miscellaneous grains. Soon there will be a shortage of food.

Jixi: Jixi County has always been known as a rice-producing area, and in previous years there was still surplus grain that was transported and sold to various places in southern She County. Last year, it suffered a severe drought, and the harvest was less than 30%. In addition, the stationed troops have recently needed a large amount of rice. Households in neighboring areas that lack grain have come to Jixi to search for it. Families that have a little surplus know that they must store it for disaster relief, but due to the needs of the end of the year, they have to sell grain to make ends meet, causing the price of rice to rise with the trend, soaring to 12 yuan per stone. Currently, the grain reserves in the city and market are very low, and prices must rise. The area around the third district has suffered bandit attacks repeatedly, and the food shortage is even more panicked. Residents of various villages have slaughtered and salted all the piglets they raised to save on food.

Xiuning: After last year's drought in Xiuning County, the harvest in the rice fields in the four rural townships was very good. There is very little grain stored in the city and rural areas, and the price of rice in the township market has soared to 12.56 to 13 yuan per stone. Poor households without land have long been digging ferns and picking dregs to survive. Even Wan'an, which is known as a rice-producing area, is experiencing a supply shortage, and the price of rice has risen from 11 yuan to 12.8 yuan. In order to relieve the future rice famine, the Xiuning County government has ordered each district to instruct rice merchants to register and quickly raise funds to transport rice from Hangzhou and Shanghai to maintain the food supply. A transport committee has been organized in the township to discuss transport regulations. Currently, rice merchants in various cities and rural areas are raising huge sums of money to purchase rice from ports and transport it to the township for assistance.

She County: After suffering a severe drought last year, the local grain reserves in She County are empty. At the beginning of the month, the price of rice soared to 14 yuan per stone. In addition, the neighboring counties have banned the export of rice, and the source is not sustainable. Merchants are using wheat flour as a substitute food, while farmers are grinding corn flour and mixing it with vegetables to make a thin soup, eating two meals a day to survive. In dozens of villages in the third district of the county, such as Xucun, Chengkan, Shangfeng, Shimen, Wangcun, and Luotian, poor people are mostly emaciated and pale, lying in the mountains and forests, digging up grass roots and bark to eat every day. Men and women in various villages in Qiankou in the fourth district go to the deep mountains every day to collect fern roots, make mountain powder to fill their stomachs, and sell them for money to make a living. (January 30)

Overview of Xuzhou's Market 87

The entire port's commerce has plummeted

There are seven reasons for the decline

Xuzhou Communication: Xuzhou Port, with its convenient transportation, has always been known for its developed commerce. Datong Street, which connects the city and the station, is especially a new commercial center. Gongqia Road has many stores with strong capital and a long history. Since the accident on Datong Street the year before last and the mutual bankruptcy of grocery stores last spring, the entire port's commerce has plummeted. At this end of the lunar year, various industries are closing down. The survey is summarized as follows:

Commercial Situation Survey 88

Xuzhou's industry is not prosperous, and residents who are considered well-off have all started out in business. Therefore, when faced with natural disasters or man-made calamities, the people's purchasing power disappears, and there is a shortage of resources. The silver and money industry is the mother of all industries. Since last year, various silver firms have not been lending money externally. The reason is that the money lent before last year is difficult to recover due to the bankruptcy of various industries. Therefore, silver merchants also feel the losses. This year, only the National Bank has a slight surplus. Other banks, such as the China Bank, the Communications Bank, and the Jiangsu Bank, are operating at a breakeven level. The local money industry, since the collapse of Gongyu and various ticket shops, has not been able to clear the debts to date. The auction of the ticket merchants' assets has also failed to attract buyers. Various ticket merchants are still sitting firmly in prison. The grocery industry largely collapsed last spring. Creditors from Shanghai firms jointly commissioned lawyer Zhu Shaowen to sit in Xuzhou and demand payment, repeatedly litigating and detaining, but there is no hope of clearing the debts. Only Shunji remains, while most others have closed down for liquidation. Only a few silk shops on Datong Street are barely surviving, attracting customers with price reductions, and the market is slightly active, but it is still outwardly strong but inwardly weak. Even Cai Yuanxing, which has the longest history, has closed down. The market for department stores is quite active, but it is only concentrated in Tiancheng, Huafeng, Taiyu, Taixiang, and other stores on Datong Street, and others are not worthy of mention. The sales of cotton yarn have always been the highest in rural areas. Since the bankruptcy of the countryside and the disappearance of farmers' purchasing power, this industry has felt the decline. Moreover, most of the goods are Japanese goods, and the supply route has been blocked, so the goods naturally feel scarce. Exhaustion is mostly competitive sales. Business, China, the world, Datong, and others have all suffered losses. The Western medicine industry has not been affected in any way. The combination of books and medicine compensates each other, but there is no profit to be made. These are all the main commercial industries in Xuzhou. Other industries, such as printing, brokerage, teahouses, and tourism, are only enough to make ends meet.

Reasons for Decline 89

The Chamber of Commerce believes that the decline in commerce this year is unprecedented. It has specifically announced the reasons for its depression: (1) The bankruptcy of the countryside is a common phenomenon in China. The United States and Europe dump their surplus food in China. China's food production cannot meet the demand, resulting in a reduction in farmers' purchasing power, which is a natural trend. (2) Xuzhou is a commercial area, not an industrial area. Since the tenth year of the Republic, although Xuzhou's commerce has been booming, it is only a selling behavior. The profit is small and the expenses are high. The past and present are very different. Without a production base, commerce has plummeted. (3) Financial depletion: The flood in the twentieth year of the Republic made people's eyes full of suffering. Finance was already insensitive. The outbreak of the Shanghai War caused the financial community to implement a tightening policy, which made the situation even more depleted. The collapse of the ticket shops made it impossible for small businesses to borrow money. The financial turnover was insensitive, and commerce fell into desperation. (4) Dumping of foreign goods: Most of the department stores in Xuzhou are Japanese goods. Since the boycott, the prices of foreign goods have fallen and dumped. Those with too many goods have not reduced half of their capital, and they are fundamentally on the verge of bankruptcy. (5) The scope of sales has shrunk: Xuzhou has always been the commercial center of northern Anhui, eastern Henan, southern Shandong, and northern Jiangsu. Since Xuzhou's economy is insensitive and there is a lack of goods, it can no longer supply the goods. The scope has shrunk, and the business is even more declining. (6) The industry rules are not complete, and the losses from pawned goods are too great: After the flood and the Shanghai War, Xuzhou merchants did not know to reduce the scope of their business and continued to borrow money to buy goods. When they could not sell the goods and were under financial pressure, they mortgaged them to the bank. At the time when the price of goods was falling, the amount of the mortgage was already small, and interest was added. Therefore, those who pawned goods lost almost all of their capital. (7) Huge expenses: The standard of living in Xuzhou has gradually increased, but the level of production has not increased. The two are weighed against each other, and the income does not cover the expenses, so they are gradually moving towards bankruptcy. The above are all the main reasons for the decline in commerce in Xuzhou.

Relief Strategies 90

After the Chamber of Commerce announced the reasons for the depression, it formulated the following relief strategies: Xuzhou's commerce is so depressed, and commerce is the backbone of Xuzhou's social organization. The situation is declining day by day, which is worrying. The Chamber of Commerce specifically announced the relief strategies to all industries: (1) For stores that are not currently bankrupt, the situation is relatively reliable. Banks should try to plan loans to facilitate turnover. (2) The banking industry's tightening is due to the loss of social credit. In the future, all stores should try to restore their reputation to strengthen the bank's credit. (3) Reduce expenses to maintain the status quo. (4) The real prosperity of Xuzhou's commerce should pay attention to the development of industry to consolidate the foundation of business. (5) Xuzhou is originally an industrial area. Foreigners are not aware of the situation in Xuzhou and have not dared to invest. The government should pay attention to the use of foreign capital and provide it with considerable guarantees. (6) The prosperity of commerce lies in the revitalization of the countryside, and the revitalization of the countryside should pay attention to production and construction. The government should especially promote and assist it. Some of the above strategies may be beyond the power of the commercial forces, so they require the expression of political forces, so that production and construction can be used as the basis for revitalization and prosperity.

Northeastern Anti-Japanese Volunteers Fighting Hard in the Severe Winter 91

Zhaoshangzhi's Troops in Yanji

Kong Xianrong's Troops in Dongning

Volunteers in Fuyu Also Active

Harbin Communication: Three years have passed since the Japanese army occupied our Northeast. The anti-Japanese volunteers in various places have fallen one after another, but the spirit of killing the enemy has not diminished. The recent situation of the volunteers fighting bravely and the activities of the Japanese and puppet troops is recorded as follows: The most active volunteers in the area along the puppet "Jingtu Line" are Zhaoshangzhi's troops. The area near Yanji has long been occupied by the volunteers. Although the Japanese and puppet police have repeatedly attacked, the volunteers have not only not suffered losses, but have been able to obtain guns and ammunition every time they fight. The Japanese and puppet troops have been repeatedly severely damaged, and they falsely accuse our volunteers of being the Red Army. It is reported that Zhaobu has only a few hundred people, but the morale is very high. The Dongning and Ning'an counties in the Suining area of the puppet Fourth Military Region have long been occupied by the volunteers' leaders Kong Xianrong, Chai Shirong, Zhong Jiusheng, Zhang Yuting, Li Sanlai, and others. There are about 10,000 volunteers in that area, and they are currently concentrating on training. Last fall, they fought with the Japanese and puppet troops several times. The Japanese army was defeated, and hundreds of puppet troops were disarmed. Therefore, the Japanese army also falsely accuses the volunteers in that area of having a considerable background. The area of Huaxin Dingzi in the Eighth District of Liaoning's Changfeng County has been recovered by the volunteers. In addition, Hailong, Qingyuan, and other county volunteers' leader Hailin led more than 400 people to Dongfeng, where the puppet troops stationed in the county went to attack. The two sides fought fiercely. The police and armor of Hu Xiantang in Hengdaohezi all assisted the puppet troops. However, the volunteers concentrated their elite troops and broke through the encirclement in the middle of the night. As a result, both sides suffered casualties. In addition, in Huanren County, there are Commander Mi, Zhan Dongbian, and Dongbian Army, who are cooperating with the Korean People's Revolutionary Army to resist Japan. The army is very strong. In addition, there are also more than 100 volunteers in Faku County, who are fighting hard against the puppet police. The leader is unknown. In the third district of Jilin's Fuyu County, more than 200 volunteers from Binjianghao, Danye, Laolaihao, Shengping, and other troops suddenly came and advanced into the seventh district. The puppet authorities have divided the military and police to defend. However, the volunteers attacked the puppet Fourth Police Station in Jiangjia Wobao in the seventh district at 6:00 AM on the 13th, and all the guns and ammunition of the more than 80 puppet police and self-defense corps were confiscated. The strength of the volunteers has greatly increased. The volunteers are planning to unite with the Dadongyang Department, which has more than 100 people, complete with guns and horses, and the number of people has increased sharply. They are planning to change their strategy to take Fuyu County to plan a major move. The Japanese puppets are setting up defenses.

Active Construction in Eastern Siberia 99

(Vladivostok Correspondence)

Mineral Development, Implementation of Electrification

In the past few centuries, especially during the Tsarist autocracy and the initial stages of the revolutionary movement, the mention of Siberia generally sent shivers down the spines of Russians, who considered it a living hell on earth. This was because Siberia had a harsh climate and a sparse population. Although the Imperial Russian government made great efforts to encourage the settlement of civilians after the completion of the Trans-Siberian Railway, the number of people who migrated there was still very small, while the number of people sentenced to exile was very large. Therefore, the general public's fear of Siberia is still quite prevalent today. The Soviet government paid special attention to Siberia during the first Five-Year Plan period, and since the beginning of the second Five-Year Plan, it has been determined to implement development. Therefore, in terms of taxation, tax rates were specially reduced, and in terms of supply, extra preferential treatment was given.

In terms of national defense, Commander of the Far Eastern Red Army Blyukher publicly stated during last year's revolutionary anniversary, "...I can assert that the Far Eastern Red Army can safeguard the peace of the motherland's borders and can firmly secure the distant borders..." Such words, on the surface, are very mild, but they strongly imply the solidity of its defense. In terms of the navy, Viktorov, Commander of the Far Eastern Navy and Chairman of the Far Eastern Naval Military Revolutionary Council, is directing the reconstruction of the Vladivostok naval port and the replenishment of submarines, preparing to cope calmly in case of emergencies. In terms of politics and economy, Larentsov is providing guidance in the name of the secretary of the Communist Party's Far Eastern Regional Committee. There is also Kirdov, Chairman of the Far Eastern Regional Executive Committee, who decides the highest guiding principles. These four people, except for Blyukher (i.e., General Galen) who is relatively well-known, are all emerging talents. It is feared that very few people abroad know about them. The Far Eastern region has a total area of approximately 2,332,000 square kilometers (five times the size of present-day Germany), while the population is only slightly more than 1.6 million. The Soviet government, recognizing the importance of the Far Eastern region, and after the September 18th Incident, even more clearly understood the dangerous situation in the Far East. Therefore, in addition to vigorously strengthening war preparations to prevent any emergencies, it further investigated the special circumstances, natural resources, and ethnic conditions of various regions, and designated the coastal province as an industrial zone within the Far Eastern region, aiming to develop its coal, iron, gold, zinc, silver, and other mineral deposits, as well as fisheries and forests.

The coastal province will use the "Bureya" coalfield as the center of its mining industry. According to experts' surveys, the coalfield has reserves of approximately 100 billion tons, making it the second-largest coalfield in the Soviet Union. After full development, not only will the ships along the Amur River use its coal, but the cities planned to be built in Khabarovsk, Komsomolsk-on-Amur, Birobidzhan, etc., will also be supplied with fuel from this coal mine. The coastal province was originally a place without a power industry, which hindered the development of general industries. Now, there are plans to build a large power plant with a generating capacity of 100,000 kilowatts (KiloWatt). The construction cost is estimated at 100 million rubles. Currently, 2,500 workers are engaged in the work, and the completion period is one year and two months.

Recently Captured Communist Bandit Leaders by the National Army 100

(Center) Su Zichang Fang Zhimin, Pseudo-Governor of the Min-Zhe-Gan Province

(Left) Liu Chouxi, Pseudo-Commander of the Tenth Army (Right) Wang Ruchih, Pseudo-Commander of the Tenth Army and Concurrent Commander of the Nineteenth Division

In terms of transportation, the Ussuri Railway did not feel the "passing trains" problem very seriously in the past because the transportation demand was not very large. However, recently, due to delays caused by "passing trains" in military and industrial development, it has been deemed very uneconomical. That's why a double track is being laid, and it will be fully completed this year. However, they are still considering the future. If an emergency occurs between the Soviet Union and Japan, the Ussuri Railway and the Trans-Siberian Railway will inevitably be cut off. Therefore, it has been decided to build the BAM Railway, connecting the northern part of Lake Baikal, the lower reaches of the Amur River, and Nikolayevsk-on-Amur. At the same time, air traffic connects Europe to Nikolayevsk-on-Amur, Sakhalin Island, and the "Chekotka" of the Arctic Ocean.

In terms of culture and education, the Far Eastern region was extremely closed in the past, but now it is gradually developing. They not only have elementary textbooks but also books like dictionaries. For example, in the coastal province, there are 135 school children for every 1,000 people, and 85% of adults are literate. There are a total of 30 specialized schools, universities, workers' preparatory courses, technical schools, factory apprentice schools, etc., with more than 8,100 students. Because of the development of natural products, the increase in population, and the improvement of cultural standards, general consumption has also increased simultaneously. In 1933, it increased by 230% compared to 1931, and from January to October 1934, it increased to 430% of 1931. However, consumer goods are still insufficient. The general social consumption power and productivity are still increasing. (January 19)

Gradual Improvement in Freight Transportation on the Wuhu-Xuancheng Section of the Jingwu Railway 101

Completion of the Dangtu River Bridge Project, Local Products Along the Route Transported to Wuhu for Export

Tunxi Correspondence: Since the construction of the Jingwu Railway by the Jiangnan Railway Company began, the progress of the project has been very rapid. Although the rainy weather for more than 20 days in early January has hindered progress to some extent, work has continued as usual without interruption. Currently, the track-laying project has reached the bank of the Dangtu River. Material vehicles travel back and forth several times a day, and passenger cars are attached to carry passengers. Three stations have been set up from Wuhu to Dangtu, and ticket sales began in the early part of the month. However, due to the transportation of materials, there is no accurate departure time, and there are few passengers. The Dangtu River Bridge project is currently 80% complete. It is being rushed day and night, and it is expected to be completed by mid-October. After the bridge is completed, not only will trains be able to pass through, but also the automobiles traveling on the Jingwu Highway will pass through, which will save the difficulty of crossing the river. As for the Wuhu-Xuancheng section, it has been open to traffic for half a year, and the business is mediocre. In addition, last year, various counties in southern Anhui suffered from drought and banditry, and the vitality of the rural areas was greatly damaged, which greatly affected the railway's business. At the beginning of the opening of freight transportation, the business was extremely light. In addition to expanding publicity in various ports along the line to promote its responsible transportation efficiency, the company also provided merchants with various conveniences. In the past two months, freight transportation has gradually improved. Xuancheng, Shuidong, Wangzhi, and other places' Xuancheng paper, tribute dates, rice, and other products are transported by train to Wuhu and then reloaded for export. Local products from Tunxi and Huining are mostly transported to Xuancheng via the Wuhu-Tunxi Road and then loaded onto trains to Wuhu. Recently, the coal from Huishan near Sunjiabu has also been transported by train. Therefore, the railway's freight transportation has been more developed than before. The freight revenue for the past two months has also gradually increased. (February 1)

The Anqing Public Security Bureau Cracked a Robbery Case 102

Bandits Shot Dead on the Spot

Anqing Correspondence: The Anhui Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau reported on the morning of the 1st that gunshots were heard outside the South Gate, according to a report from the Nan River Patrol Police Station. The station chief immediately ordered Inspector Zhang Rujia and Detective Team Leader Xie Lizhong to lead team members and police officers to rush to the scene, and also telegraphed Qian Ruiting, the director of the Second Branch Bureau, to lead the police to take action. It was immediately discovered that bandits were robbing Yuan Yinji's plaster shop at No. 9 Xicheng Street outside the South Gate. When asked about the shopkeeper's son, he claimed that the bandit was about thirty years old, spoke with a Hanshan County accent, and had two gold teeth. After entering the shop, he turned around and closed the door, holding a pistol in his hand, and forbade anyone to make a sound. He claimed that he was short of travel expenses and had come to borrow 100 yuan. He immediately ordered the money counter to be opened, and took away all the bank notes inside: one 5-yuan note from the Bank of China, two 5-yuan notes from the Central Bank, 7 or 8 yuan in silver dollars, three 1-yuan notes, and about 1 yuan in small denomination notes. He fired a shot when he left, and the bullet hit the counter. After the bandit left the shop, he fired three more shots as a warning and fled towards Xicheng Lane. At that time, the residents along the street were extremely frightened, and the shopkeeper's son followed behind the bandit, shouting "Catch the thief!" The police officers on duty followed and chased after him. It happened that police officer Huang Yezeng of the Second Branch Bureau encountered the bandit in Xicheng Lane and intercepted him. The bandit fired several shots in a row, and the bandit also returned fire. The bandit was shot dead on the spot. A divorce document was found on the bandit's body, with the name Cao Xulai, a native of Hanshan County, residing in Wuhu. There was also an eight-shot pistol, four bullets, and more than 20 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars robbed from Yuan Yinji's shop. (February 2)

The Shandong Construction Department Establishes a Tobacco Leaf Experiment Station 103

Members Have Been Sent to Xindian to Purchase Land

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Construction Department, recognizing that the province's tobacco leaf industry is declining and needs to be improved, has decided to establish a tobacco leaf experiment station in Xindian, Linzi. Jia Xueqi and Sun Chongxin have been appointed to purchase 300 acres of land and prepare for the establishment of the experiment station. Jia and others will depart from Jinan in the coming days to Xindian to purchase land. In addition, the Construction Department recently sent technician Chen Shican to Shanghai to negotiate a silk loan with the Shanghai Bank. Chen has sent a letter to Jinan, stating that he has met with Director Zhang (Honglie) in Shanghai, and the silk loan has been agreed upon with the Shanghai Bank. He will return to Jinan soon. It is said that the amount of the loan is approximately more than 100,000 yuan.

Songjiang

Official Correspondence Regarding the Accommodation of Zhejiang Disaster Victims 104

Since Zhejiang suffered a drought disaster last year, about 2,000 refugees have been stranded in Songjiang. The Songjiang Red Cross Society, witnessing this miserable situation, gathered local comrades and established a shelter at Chao Gu Temple. It has been accommodating refugees for days, with already 1,300 to 1,400 people. The management is gradually taking shape. The county government's official letters to the relief institute are listed below: (1) Letter from the Songjiang County Relief Institute: Responding directly: "Upon receiving your society's Letter No. 7, which states, 'To whom it may concern, recently, disaster victims from Zhejiang Province have been arriving in Songjiang in an endless stream, all without clothing or food. Our society, witnessing this miserable situation, cannot bear to sit idly by. Therefore, we plan to establish a temporary shelter for Zhejiang drought disaster refugees. We have decided to start accommodating them at Songjiang Chao Guo Temple on the 31st of this month. Your institute aims to provide relief and shares the same charitable goal as our society. We dare to write to request your assistance at any time and also request a copy of the situation of the disaster victims in Songjiang and the register of disaster victims, so that we can learn from it. We are extremely grateful,' etc. Approved. Upon investigation, refugees from western Zhejiang are fleeing famine to Songjiang one after another. The gentlemen of your society, feeling the suffering in their hearts, continue to provide accommodation, and their enthusiasm for charity is deeply admired. Our institute has been distributing rice and money at the Third District Public Security Branch Station since the 8th of this month, and has been distributing bread at the Sacrifice River Pavilion since the 21st. As for the number of disaster victims in Songjiang, it is at most more than 1,000 people per day, and at least 500 people. However, there are frequent comings and goings, so the number also increases or decreases from time to time. Correspondingly, we reply to the letter and hope that you will check it. Sincerely, Li Zuhua, Director of the Songjiang Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society, Sun Shiheng, Deputy Director." (2) Letter from the Songjiang County Government: According to your society's Letter No. 6, a request was made to establish a shelter at Chao Guo Temple to accommodate drought disaster refugees from Zhejiang Province passing through, requesting a notice of protection and transferring it to the Public Security Bureau to send police to guard and take care of them, and to send all Zhejiang refugees to the shelter, etc., demonstrating enthusiasm and determination, and benefiting the victims. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to handle it, a proclamation has been specially drafted and sent to you for review. This is to the Songjiang Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society, County Magistrate Jin Tigan.

Old Father Died After Being Robbed at the End of the Year 105

Yang Xingqin's family, a farmer in Dongyu Village, Zhangjiawan Township, Qitu, Tianma Mountain, was broken into by eight or nine bandits at 12:00 on the night of the 31st of last month. They robbed three and a half stones of white rice, 3,000 copper coins, New Year's cakes, fresh meat, and other items. Before leaving, they hit Yang Xingqin's biological father, Jiang Defu, with an iron bamboo shoot shovel, piercing his skull, and he died instantly. The next day, the Tianma Mountain Branch Station was informed, which reported it to the County Public Security Bureau, which sent detectives to investigate. Fei Gongxia, the captain of the Water Patrol Team, also went to investigate and questioned the victim in detail about the process. Yang's relative, Lai Pi A Bu, had a recent quarrel with Jiang Defu, and it was believed that A Bu was highly suspected. A Bu was arrested in Songjiang and sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. However, according to A Bu's statement, on the night of the incident, he stayed at a certain family's house in Songcheng. Further investigation is pending.

Thorough Investigation of the Case of Private Possession of Military Firearms and Opium 106

According to a confidential report to the County Government, the township head of Fengjing Jiezizhen Township, surnamed Pan, was suspected of privately possessing military firearms and selling opium. A team was sent to search, and 39 rounds of quick-firing bullets, a package of stamped official opium, and multiple packages of private opium were found. The township head Pan was taken back to the County Government for interrogation on the 3rd. According to his statement, the bullets were left over from the previous militia regiment, and the opium was deducted from the rent owed by a tenant who opened a smoking den. However, Pan is addicted to opium, and he was ordered to be sent to a drug rehabilitation center for detoxification before further investigation.

Adultery and Wife Murder Case Sentenced 107

Zhang Xiaohe, a resident of Deshenggang Township, had an affair with his sister-in-law, Zhang Shen. He killed his legal wife, Ye, with a kitchen knife, inflicting as many as thirteen wounds. Her throat was cut and her hand fell off, which was unbearable to hear. The victim's mother filed a complaint with the court. After repeated interrogations, the defendant hired a lawyer to defend him. Yesterday (the 5th), the court, with Judge Zhang Yihuang presiding, announced the verdict, sentencing Zhang Xiaohe and Zhang Shen to ten years of imprisonment each for their crime of murder, as a warning to others.

Suzhou

Tragic Fire at the Fire Brigade 108

The No. 5 Fire Brigade in the northern section of Taibo Temple Bridge in the Cangmen area of Suzhou City caught fire at 3:30 PM on the afternoon of the 5th. Due to the carelessness of a certain staff member, gasoline was accidentally ignited, causing a fire. The fire immediately broke through the roof, and the flames illuminated the sky. Fortunately, the nearby fire brigade was notified and rushed to the rescue, and the fire was quickly extinguished. When the fire was raging, Shen Chunzhi, who was guarding the fire station, was burned to death because he could not escape in time. Yesterday (the 6th), after the local prosecutor's office sent personnel to investigate, they immediately ordered that a coffin be prepared for burial.

Smoked to Death in a Robbery Case in Huguan 109

The Gu family, a farmer in Hushu Pass, Suzhou, about three miles from the town, had considerable assets, so they were coveted by bandits. On the night of the last day of the lunar year, many bandits suddenly came with weapons to rob. They tied up the victim, Mr. Gu, and smoked his lower body with fire, forcing him to reveal the location of the hidden money. Unexpectedly, Mr. Gu was smoked to death. The bandits then began to search and rob, and took away the stolen goods. The next day, the local Bao reported to the local court, which sent personnel to verify that Mr. Gu had indeed been burned to death alive. They ordered the family to prepare a coffin for burial and await the arrest and investigation of the murderer.

Wuxi 110

Discovery of the Coffin of Di Qing of the Song Dynasty

Townspeople in Huangtutang Town, District 7 of this county, automatically dredged the river in the town for the sake of planning for this spring before the rains, due to the severe drought last summer. Unexpectedly, when plowing the mud at the bottom of the river, they suddenly could not plow down, and there was a clanging sound on the ground. They loosened the surrounding mud and dug at the place where the sound came from, and found a huge red coffin, more than fifteen feet long, five feet wide, and as high as a person's shoulders. One end of the coffin was engraved with the twelve characters "The Coffin of General Di Qing, Grand Chancellor of the Song Dynasty", and the coffin wood from time to time emits a strange fragrance, presumed to be made of Agarwood. The townspeople were shocked and happy. They uncovered the lid to examine it, but unexpectedly, there were no clothes, quilts, or corpses inside, only two jade cups, crystal clear and lovely. According to Di Qing, he was from Xihe in the Northern Song Dynasty, known as Han Chen. He was proficient in military strategy and repeatedly made military exploits during the reign of Emperor Renzong, and was appointed as the Privy Councilor and Grand Chancellor. After his death, he was given the posthumous title of Wu Xiang and was once granted jade mandarin ducks. The above-mentioned jade cups may be the jade mandarin ducks that have been passed down from generation to generation, but the words of unofficial historians should not be taken as complete evidence.

Sudden Snowfall After the Beginning of Spring 111

Since the beginning of winter in this county, the weather has been warm, and the Fahrenheit thermometer has been above 50 degrees, and there has been no snowfall. The farmers are quite worried. The day before yesterday was the Beginning of Spring Festival, and the temperature was even higher. Walking in a fur coat felt sweaty and breathless. At the same time, the sky was blue, and the breeze was gentle and the sun was bright. Chong'an Temple and other places were filled with an endless stream of tourists. The business of various entertainment venues was also quite good. Yesterday, after dawn, the weather turned cold, and the thermometer dropped to 44 degrees. From 8:00 AM, snow suddenly began to fall, and after 9:00 AM, it became slightly larger, mixed with drizzle. The sky was covered with dark clouds, indicating a heavy snowfall.

Inspecting the Cars on the Xi-Cheng Road 112

The Xi-Cheng Long-Distance Bus Company has repeatedly caused disasters due to outdated vehicles and negligent employees. It is learned that the Jiangsu Provincial Highway Administration, in order to rectify the situation, has advanced the inspection of the Xi-Cheng Long-Distance Bus Association in the two counties of Xishan and Jiangyin. Also, in the case of the Jiangnan Motor Company restricting the passage of small cars on the Xi-Yi Road, the Administration and the Construction Bureau of this county replied yesterday that before the new measures are approved, the company should continue to operate according to the licensed number of seats and must not illegally obstruct them.

Changzhou 113

Overview of the Closure of Various Industries at the End of the Lunar Year

After last year's drought disaster in Wujin County, the rural economy was on the verge of bankruptcy, purchasing power was weak, and business was declining, presenting an unprecedented situation. It was already difficult to barely maintain and pass through peacefully. During this period, closures due to poor turnover and losses were frequently heard. The best performance among industries was beans and cotton, which were able to make a profit under such a bleak situation. The bean industry had already made a considerable profit in 1933. In 1934, the goods arriving by land and water were extremely crowded, all concentrated in the Dou Shihe area, and the trading was very extensive. Regardless of the size of the firms, all had a surplus. As for local cotton, which is produced in Wujin County, factories have been established in recent years to improve production, and the factory cloth produced has been increasing year by year, and the distant ones are sold to the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong. Last year, the industry worked hard and the business was booming, so it was able to make a profit at the end of the year. Other industries, such as wood, oil mills, and rice, had a slight profit. The silk and foreign goods industries suffered from low prices and high expenses, and some suffered losses and closures. The clothing industry found it difficult to maintain due to cheap silk cloth and outdated inventory. As for the money shops, they have all closed down since the January 28th Incident. Last year, only HSBC, Hongxiang, and Taicheng remained, and there was no surplus profit to be made. It is feared that it will be difficult to maintain this year. With the decline of money shops, banks have risen. In addition to the branches established by foreign banks, Wujin Bank, which is in this county, has been open for only a little over a year and already has a profit to speak of.

Zhenjiang 114

Registration of Household Registration in Lawsuits

The Provincial Government recently announced to the counties of Jiangbei that most of the Baojia system has been completed, and the counties of Jiangnan are also in the process of implementation. It specially instructed all counties and requested the Higher Court to forward the instructions for compliance. From now on, when the people file lawsuits with the government and autonomous organs, or enter into contracts with each other, they must register their household registration in the nationality column in accordance with the current Baojia organization (for example, the number of districts, townships, Bao, Jia, and households in a certain county) in order to train the general public to recognize the importance of the Baojia and further understand the close relationship between the government and each other.

Drought Relief Donations Received More Than 60,000 Yuan 115

As of the end of last month, the Zhenjiang County Drought Relief Association has received a total of more than 60,000 yuan in donations, including 33,068 yuan from Shanghai, 800 yuan from Beiping, 1,000 yuan from Nanjing, 530 yuan from Bengbu, 900 yuan from Zhengzhou, 11,034 yuan from Zhenjiang, 18,234 yuan from house rentals, and 1,071 yuan, 3 corners, and 4.5 points from movie donations. Although the above numbers are not small, they are still far from the original budget. As for the work relief projects undertaken by the association, the first, second, and fourth districts have already started construction on some parts, the third and sixth districts are being organized, and the fifth district is still being reviewed. It is estimated that it will not be possible to start construction on all projects until mid-February.

Ningbo 116

Security Branch Executes Five Pirates by Firing Squad

Five pirates, Hua Zhongxian, Chen Meixian, Chen A Luo, Yang Simei, and Chen Meijie, and the bandit leader San Laoda and others, gathered in the Donglang Sea Mountain area of the former Taiwan jurisdiction, resisted government troops, robbed passing merchant ships, and kidnapped as many as thirty-eight or nine passengers. They hid in the Donglang Mountain cave. In July of this year, the Yongping warship of the Water Police Team, together with the Linhai Cadre Team, went to encircle and suppress them. The bandits resisted stubbornly, injuring six police officers and water police. Subsequently, the Water Police and others launched a fierce attack, killing seven bandits at the time, capturing Hua Zhongxian and others alive, and rescuing thirty-eight refugees. After the bandits were captured, they were sent to the Second Security Branch and sentenced to death according to law. Yesterday (the 31st), upon receiving the order from Chairman Chiang, the branch immediately extracted the bandits Hua Zhongxian and others and tied them to Fengcao Horse Road in Jiangbei for execution by firing squad.

The Scene at the Start of the Abandoned Lunar Year

Here, various businesses, except for teahouses and the like, followed the usual practice of closing for three days at the start of the abandoned lunar year. The three banks in the North City—China, Local, and Farmers—also closed for three days. Theaters opened everywhere, and due to the clear weather and low prices, most were fully booked. As for the overall financial outcome of businesses in the Jiaxu year, according to investigations, accounts received only amounted to sixty to seventy percent. Zou Boyang, a revenue officer from the Third District Revenue Bureau, suddenly disappeared on February 2nd, just as the bureau was about to settle tax payments.
