Hefei 121

Post Office Remittance Department Director Flees with Large Sum of Money

Wang Pingkun, from Huaining, aged over thirty, the director of the remittance department of the Hefei Post Office, had incurred significant debts while serving as the postmaster of the Sanhe Post Office due to excessive indulgence. After being transferred to the Hefei Post Office, he embezzled public funds. When the new postmaster Qi Rongqing took office and began working diligently, Wang feared exposure and punishment. Taking advantage of the Lunar New Year season, when businesses in the city were remitting large sums of money to various ports along the Yangtze River for settlement, on January 29th, he suddenly fled with over 21,000 silver dollars. His mother, wife, and five children also left the area at the same time. Postmaster Qi Rongqing was shocked upon discovering this and immediately telegraphed the Postal Administration Bureau, which forwarded the report to the Ministry of Transportation, notifying the governments of all provinces and ordering all cities and counties to conduct thorough searches of arriving passengers to prevent anyone from escaping. At the same time, he notified the local military and government authorities to conduct a strict search. The county government has ordered the First District Office to conduct a census of the entire city. So far, he has not been found. It is reported that Wang had received a letter from a friend at a post office outside the customs pass a few days earlier, urging him to go there. Wang may have fled outside the customs pass this time.

Spring Snow Fell in the City Yesterday 129

Since the beginning of winter, the weather in the city has been very mild, with temperatures often around forty degrees. Not only has there been no ice or snow, but there have also been frequent heavy fogs. The weather was clear on the day before yesterday (i.e., the Lunar New Year's Day), as warm as mid-spring. After the Beginning of Spring on Tuesday (commonly called the second day of the New Year), the weather suddenly changed, with a piercing north wind, which became even stronger in the evening, blowing harder and harder. After midnight, it turned into a northeast wind. In the morning, the sky was overcast. Around 2:00 PM, it began to rain, gradually becoming denser and mixed with snowflakes. Around 3:00 PM, the snowflakes became larger, but because the weather during the day was not very cold, although it rained and snowed all day, there was no accumulation.

Two Ship Collision Cases; Jianguo Undergoing Inspection and Repair 130

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jianguo steamer, on its way to Hankou, collided with the E Jian Ying Fu Chu tugboat on the Jiangsha River near Xiaogushan, causing significant damage. This matter was briefly noted in this newspaper's extra edition. Later, Jianguo returned to Shanghai, where the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent personnel to inspect it. The guardrails on the port side of the deck were completely destroyed, totaling four places, over 100 feet. The iron plates outside the coal bunker were also damaged, screws were loosened, and a hole was punched in the hull. The engine in the engine room was also shaken, and the keel suffered collateral damage. This matter was first verified and recorded by the Hankou Shipping Administration Bureau and has now been transferred to Hankou for negotiation. Jianguo has been suspended from service and is undergoing major repairs in Hankou. The company has informed the Zhaotai Insurance Company of the various losses and the circumstances of the accident for their review.

Inventor of Rejuvenation Technique, Russian Doctor Arrives in Shanghai 134

He is 65 Years Old

Married Just Last Year

According to the North China Daily News, Dr. Voronoff, a renowned surgeon who invented the rejuvenation technique of grafting ape gonads into humans, has arrived in Shanghai and is staying at the Cathay Hotel. The doctor is 65 years old and full of energy. Born in Russia, he moved to Paris at the age of 17. He speaks fluent English when talking to people. The doctor said, "I have been engaged in experiments for many years. I believe that it is a mistake for doctors to only treat diseases. Old age and physical weakness should be strengthened, and the inability of men and women of middle age to resist diseases is not a good sign. Look at the newspapers, famous people aged 65 to 70 often die in winter. This is because they are unable to resist the cold. Once their physical strength declines, any accident can kill them, which is inevitable. Therefore, they die. My entire work is to restore people's normal life expectancy. If we can repair the human body like repairing a car, replacing old parts with new ones, then we can achieve this goal. You cannot replace the brain or heart with new ones, but you can replace the mechanism that operates these organs. Glands without transporting tubes are the mechanism that controls the so-called essential organs. We can replace these glands with new ones because the problem lies with the glands themselves, not the heart of the glands. Only the heart may be diseased, but if healthy, it can last forever." The doctor continued, saying that after many years of experimentation, he performed the first experiment on humans in 1920, grafting the gonads of healthy apes into humans. The result was to increase human lifespan, eliminate some deep wrinkles, strengthen the necessary resistance to disease, and make people energetic. After five or six years, a 70-year-old man who has undergone the procedure looks like he is about 50 years old and feels that way himself. However, after six years, the procedure must be performed again. Therefore, the number of times the procedure is performed to maintain health cannot be limited. After continuing to research, he discovered that in addition to the gonads, there are other things that maintain youthfulness. The adrenal glands and thyroid gland also play a major role in human decline. Five years ago, he discovered the classification of ape blood, which is the same as human blood. However, ape blood only contains the third and fourth types. Therefore, men and women belonging to the first or second blood types cannot benefit from the procedure. When asked by reporters about the success rate of the procedure, the doctor replied that only five or six out of a hundred people who adhere to all the rules of the procedure and are thorough without any omissions can obtain absolute and satisfactory results. Healthy life can be extended for 10 to 12 years. The doctor also explained that removing the thyroid gland will result in idiocy, and removing the adrenal glands will immediately stop the heart. Therefore, grafting these three glands can restore the strength of the human body through the action of the heart and brain. Reporters then asked why the effect of the surgery does not last long. The doctor replied that humans can only imitate the Creator. God created a complete vascular tissue to nourish the organs and glands of the human body, reaching every pore. We cannot imitate this so completely. Therefore, when the blood vessels we graft into the human body have completed their work, the glands with insufficient nutrition will lose their function and must be operated on again. Reporters asked the doctor to try his skills while staying in Shanghai. The doctor and his wife both smiled. The doctor concluded, "We were married eight months ago and are currently on our honeymoon tour. After leaving Shanghai, we will also travel to Japan and the United States."

Shanghai-Minhang Long-Distance Phone Service Opened

Finance Minister Kong Talks About the Currency Advisory Committee 136

Reuters, Shanghai, 6th: Last week, it was widely reported in the city that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission convened an important meeting in Beijing to draft a plan to immediately reform China's currency and financial system. Reuters issued a news report on January 31st stating that the authorities denied such news. According to the highest authority, not only was no such meeting held, but the claim that a Currency Advisory Committee had been established as a result of this meeting was also incorrect. In fact, this action was decided by the Minister of Finance several months ago and was not the result of the Finance Minister's recent visit to Beijing. A Reuters reporter interviewed Finance Minister Kong in Shanghai, who said that he decided to appoint a Currency Advisory Committee several months ago to establish a regular body so that the Finance Minister could at any time seek the opinions of leading bankers in the country. The committee has only recently been formed and has not yet put forward concrete recommendations on the specific actions to be taken to deal with the current financial situation, nor has it developed a plan to reform the currency system. Outside reports about the relationship of the appointment of this Advisory Committee are clearly exaggerated. Even if the committee makes suggestions on currency reform in the future, it is impossible to predict what decisions the central government will make at this time. Any decision on this matter will depend on the situation.

It is now known that supervisor Shu Chushi went to Beijing on the 2nd of this month to seek instructions from the Executive Yuan regarding the shipment of antiques to England, so that they can be selected for shipment to England to participate in the exhibition. According to someone at the office yesterday, since Mr. Shu left Shanghai, the work of inspecting the antiques has been temporarily suspended, and it is said that Mr. Shu will come to Shanghai in a day or two to continue the work.

Jianghai Customs Proclamation on Measures to Suppress Unlicensed Silver Transportation 141

Jianghai Customs issued Proclamation No. 1426 yesterday, stating that measures to suppress the smuggling of silver coins or silver-related exports have been repeatedly proclaimed by the customs. Now, the Ministry of Finance has ordered the following provisions for rewarding and punishing the seizure of smuggled silver coins or silver-related exports: (1) Smuggled silver coins or silver-related exports seized will be confiscated, and a fine equal to double the amount of the smuggled amount will be imposed. Those who instigate the smuggling will be severely punished. (2) After the confiscated silver coins or silver-related exports are sold, bonuses will be awarded according to the following methods: A. If the seizure is made solely by customs or military and police agencies, the bonus will be doubled according to the customs' reward method for those without informants, that is, 60% will be awarded for extraordinary merit and 40% for ordinary merit. For example, if 10,000 silver coins are smuggled and seized, military police or customs officers with extraordinary merit will be awarded 6,000 yuan, and those with ordinary merit will be awarded 4,000 yuan. B. If customs receive information from an informant and the seizure is made with the assistance of military and police agencies, the bonus will be doubled according to the customs' reward method for those with informants. Military police and informants will each receive 40%, and customs officers will receive 20%. In the previous example, military police and informants will each receive 4,000 yuan, and customs officers will receive 2,000 yuan. C. If customs receive information from an informant and the seizure is made without the assistance of military and police agencies, the informant will receive 60% and customs officers will receive 40%. D. If customs make the seizure with the assistance of military and police agencies but without information from an informant, the military police will receive 40% and customs officers will receive 40%. The names of the informants should be kept confidential. (3) The fine equal to double the amount stipulated in the first item, except where the smuggler has escaped and cannot be punished or the smuggler is unable to pay the fine, will be awarded at a rate of 20% each to the military police, informants, and customs officers related to categories A, B, C, and D in the second item, and the remainder will be turned over to the government. These provisions must be followed and will be implemented from January 15th of this year. However, the reward and punishment measures do not apply to smuggled silver subsidiary coins in domestic ports seized by customs or military and police agencies. The bonus for military and police agencies should be regarded as a collective and distributed accordingly, not issued to the military and police agencies separately in the prescribed amounts. This is hereby proclaimed.

Arrested in Shenzhuang, Pudong on the 2nd

Ministry of Finance Emphasizes Supervision of Financial Institution Registration 144

Strict Suppression of Unregistered Institutions

Prior Filing Required for Branch Establishment

Ta Kung Pao reports that although most banks and financial institutions established by merchants and people in various provinces and cities have applied for registration according to regulations to be supervised and directed by the government, some are still hesitant and may violate government orders. To emphasize supervision, the Ministry of Finance has compiled a detailed list of banks, native banks, financial companies, and trust companies that have been approved for registration, and has sent notices to the provincial and municipal governments to instruct their respective competent authorities to conduct thorough investigations. Any unregistered banks, native banks, financial companies, or trust companies should be ordered to register with the Ministry of Finance immediately, while supervision should continue at all times. As for banks and companies that have already been approved for registration, if they establish branches in various provinces and cities, they should submit films of documents approved by the Ministry to the local government for review and filing. Those who establish branches without approval from the Ministry should be reported to the Ministry by the local government for investigation and handling to be suppressed. This collaborative effort aims to ensure comprehensive supervision of financial operations, to provide reliable protection for the people's economy. The municipal government of this city has already received the Ministry of Finance's notice and has instructed the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to pay attention to investigation and reporting at all times.

Railway Bureau Builds Office Buildings for the North Station 148

Decision Made at the Baoshan Road Intersection

Borrowing from the Pension Savings Fund

The headquarters of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration was originally at the Shanghai North Station. After being destroyed in the January 28th Incident in 1932, it temporarily rented office space, incurring huge annual rental costs. Furthermore, some departments were scattered in other locations, making communication inconvenient. In the autumn of the previous year, there was a proposal to rebuild the headquarters. The Ministry of Railways sent personnel to survey the site, with the principle of utilizing the existing railway land to save land purchase costs. Three locations were surveyed: one near the Maigen Road freight station, one at the Baoshan Road intersection, and one near the Shanghai West Station (i.e., Fanwangdu Station). The Baoshan Road location was the most suitable for management due to its connection with the current North Station. The Shanghai West Station location had the best environment and convenient transportation. The Maigen Road location was inferior in terms of both environment and transportation. After discussion, it was decided to use the Baoshan Road intersection as the new headquarters site. In terms of funding, it was negotiated that the Pension Savings Fund Committee of the two railways would allocate 700,000 yuan, which would be repaid annually with principal and interest using the current rental costs of the Riverside Mansion. At the same time, the bureau negotiated with the China-British Bank for agreement. Dong Dayou, an architect, was hired to be responsible for the architectural design and supervision of the project. A contract has been signed, and Deputy Director Pu and Director Ying have been designated as representatives for coordination, with specific responsibilities. However, the land at the Baoshan Road intersection was originally leased to the Shengshun Company to build the Shengshun Lane houses for rent. According to the lease agreement, negotiations were held with the company to recover a portion of the leased land, with an area of ​​approximately three mu. Recently, both parties reached an agreement. Due to the construction of the bureau's office, the old houses that need to be demolished include six three-story buildings, numbered 9, 39, 47, 53, 59, and 65, and seven two-story buildings, numbered 10, 19, 20, 21, 22, 23, and 24. All of them will be purchased by the railway bureau at an estimated price according to the contract and returned by the end of March. A portion of the purchase price has already been paid, and the Shengshun Company has notified all tenants to vacate before the end of March. Therefore, the railway bureau expects construction of the new headquarters to begin in April of this year.

Last Year's Tung Oil Exports Increased Sharply 152

Commodity Inspection Bureau Releases Report on Reasons

The Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, considering that Chinese merchants have not paid attention to improving the quality of foreign trade and often adulterate goods, resulting in a decline in reputation, has specially followed the inspection procedures and requires all export goods to be inspected separately according to the regulations. Last year, after the Bureau's inspection of tung oil, the report showed that exports accounted for 100,000 metric tons, or about 160,000 dan in the old unit, which is the most seen in history. In 1933, it was 33,000 dan, which had increased by more than three times compared to 1932. Last year, it exceeded four or five times. The reasons released by the Commodity Inspection Bureau are recorded as follows: Last year, Zhejiang produced more tung oil, totaling 160,000 to 170,000 dan. However, due to the impact of rural bankruptcy, domestic sales were sluggish, and the spring market price was 3 to 4 yuan lower than in Hankou. Therefore, foreign merchants purchased Zhejiang oil in Shanghai, and the export volume was therefore larger than in previous years. Subsequently, due to the reduction in inventory in Shanghai and Hangzhou, the price began to resemble Hankou in June and July. In August and September, the Shipping Industry Europe-America Association reduced freight rates, and foreign merchants took the opportunity to purchase, and the market price rose to 33.6 yuan. In October, freight rates increased, exports were scarce, and the market price was also flat, falling to 28 yuan. However, there was not much inventory in the producing areas, so there were not many transactions. In November, new oil was put on the market. Due to drought, the harvest was generally only 50% to 60%. Most of the arrived goods had insufficient refractive index and could not pass the inspection for export, so oil merchants did not dare to sell. Foreign firms only traded slightly. The prices in Hankou and Changde were therefore low. This is the general reason for the increase in tung oil exports last year compared to previous years.

One-Yuan Quarrel Leads to Fatal Stabbing 162

Wang Murders Yongde over Drinking Spree

Yongde Dies Unjustly

Jiang Yongtai and Yongde, two brothers from Shandong Province living at No. 19, Lane 60, Yangjiazhai, Pudong, are both laborers at the Xiangsheng Iron Factory in Lujiazui. At 6:00 p.m. on the 2nd of this month, they were invited by a friend surnamed Zhang to Zhang's house for New Year's Eve dinner. Yongde also brought his son. Yongtai, because of his nephew, gave Yongde's son two silver dollars as New Year's money. The child was only ten years old and was playing with the silver dollars in his hand when he suddenly lost one dollar. Yongde discovered this and looked for it with a candle, but to no avail. At that time, Wang Dui, another Shandong native who worked in the same factory as Yongde and was known to him, was also present. He was drunk from drinking and was very unhappy to see Yongde searching for it. He thought that one yuan was not worth making such a fuss about. He scolded Yongde with harsh words. Yongde had no place to vent his anger and became even more resentful when he heard this. The two started arguing, then fighting. Wang Dui felt that he was losing out and left in a rage. He went outside to get a knife and ran back to retaliate. He happened to see Yongde standing at the door and, taking him by surprise, slashed Yongde on the left face, cutting deep into his brain. Yongde was injured and fell to the ground. Wang saw that he had achieved his goal and ran away without a trace. Yongtai quickly sent his injured brother to Pudong Hospital for treatment. Due to his serious injuries, he died late at night. After the incident, the Third Detachment of the police was informed and sent police to Wang's house to wait. At 1:00 a.m., Wang suddenly sneaked home and was caught and taken to the Pudong Public Security Bureau for questioning. The next morning, the bureau summoned the local guarantor, Lu Shunlong, to report to the local court. After sending someone to inspect the body, he ordered the body to be handed over to the family for collection. The murderer, Wang Dui, was sent to court for legal proceedings.

However, this preparation requires a lot of labor and may take a month to complete.

Huamei Launches This Year's Longevity Brand Name Brand Cigarettes 164

China Huamei Tobacco Company has always been praised for revitalizing industry and serving society. Its Guanghua, Maisigan, and Ginseng brand cigarettes have long been popular and widely sold. Last year, the company's General Manager, Jing Yimeng, returned after inspecting the national goods industry throughout the country. He realized that although domestic cigarettes had produced various grades to meet the needs of society, there was still a lack of high-end cigarettes, which was not a way to promote domestic goods and plug the leaks. Therefore, the company collected the most expensive raw materials and used scientific methods to manufacture "Longevity Brand" name brand cigarettes, taking the meaning of "Happy Flowers, Full Moon, Longevity and Abundant Harvest." The tobacco silk of this cigarette is yellow and tender, the taste is sweet, and the golden decoration is the top grade of domestic cigarettes.

Telephone Bills to Be Paid Monthly 165

Implemented from April 1st

Shanghai Telephone Company sent a letter to all users yesterday, which stated, "Dear users, please be informed that the company has decided to implement the monthly calculation and distribution of bills from April 1, 1935. This is to notify you that all bills will be sent once a month in the future, instead of quarterly as before. This change in billing method has been approved by the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession and the French Municipal Council. In order to implement this change, all user bills must be paid up to March 31, 1935. Therefore, the telephone fee on the attached bill refers to the cost of two months from February 1st to March 31st. In other words, the amount listed is two-thirds of the usual quarterly fee currently in effect. The bill will also list the amount of the quarterly fee (for reference) and the amount of silver dollars payable for two months. The company believes that this new method will be more convenient for users than the current method." Shanghai Telephone Company, February 1, 1935.

(Shanghai Municipal New Life Group Wedding Regulations)

(1) Application for Registration: (1) Any citizen of this city holding a wedding ceremony may apply to participate in the group wedding ceremony. Inauguration of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association Headquarters Yesterday 172

More than 80 people including Chinese Director Yuan Lvdeng attended

Macy Reports on the Organization's Progress and Mission

According to Xin Xin News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession, together with rickshaw merchants and pullers, organized the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association, which held its opening ceremony at the headquarters on Dong Jiaxing Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. A total of more than 80 people attended, including the association's directors Macy, Wang Zhiren, Zhu Cheng, Yin Zhiling, Chinese Director Yuan Lvdeng, and rickshaw puller representatives. The details are recorded as follows:

Opening Ceremony 173

The venue was located in the auditorium of the headquarters on the upper floor of the small vegetable market at the intersection of Dong Jiaxing Road and Fengtian Road. A horizontal banner reading "Inauguration Ceremony of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association" was hung in front of the door. In the middle of the auditorium were hung the national flag of China and the association's emblem. Flags of various countries around the world were hung around the perimeter, and the stage was decorated with flowers and trees. The arrangement was neat. Around 2:00 PM, the directors and rickshaw pullers arrived one after another, and the ceremony began. First, Chairman Macy reported on the progress of the organization, followed by speeches by Chinese Director Yuan Lvdeng, Shanghai University President Liu Zhanen, and YMCA General Secretary Lu Ganchen. Finally, rickshaw puller representative Zhu Liuhe gave a speech. The meeting adjourned around 4:00 PM.

Opening of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association Headquarters (Photo by Wang Kai)

Chairman's Report 174

Chairman Macy's report briefly stated: "Distinguished guests, I am extremely pleased that you have attended today's opening ceremony of the headquarters of this association. On behalf of the board of directors of this association, I would like to express my welcome and gratitude to everyone. The origins of this association can be traced back to July of last year, when the Public Concession's Rickshaw Affairs Committee wanted to improve the lives of public rickshaw pullers, because their lives were extremely painful and they did not enjoy the welfare that human beings in modern civilized society should enjoy. This situation was explained in great detail in the report of the Rickshaw Research Committee published by the Public Concession a year ago. The Rickshaw Affairs Committee was entrusted by the board of directors of the Public Concession to be responsible for the implementation of the recommendations of the Rickshaw Research Committee approved by the board of directors. There are still many problems at present, but today my purpose is not to report to you in detail how much the committee has done on the recommendations of the Rickshaw Research Committee, or how much is yet to be done, and what it hopes to do in the future, but rather what the purpose of the committee's initiation of this association is. The Rickshaw Affairs Committee felt that it had the mission of planning to improve the lives of rickshaw pullers and should establish a social insurance plan to reduce the suffering of rickshaw pullers and their families due to injuries. Although there are already many charitable organizations in the concession that are also engaged in this type of work, most of them are limited by their financial resources and can only touch on the periphery. At the same time, we feel that to accomplish anything, we must have reliable funding, so we have decided that the only way is to take it out of the pockets of those who benefit. In general, this seems difficult to implement, but it so happened that the establishment of this association coincided with the Public Concession's reduction of rickshaw rents. Because the Public Concession decided at that time that the daily rickshaw rent must be reduced by about 25%, we thought that it might be possible for the rickshaw pullers to take out a certain amount of money from their own pockets every day to manage welfare services for them. However, most rickshaw pullers lack knowledge, and it is difficult to ask them to organize themselves and manage their own affairs, so we also thought that others should help them and manage things they cannot do themselves. Speaking of which, I feel very happy that the Public Concession thought of the benefits of establishing this association at that time, resolutely and happily advocated compliance, and was willing to help collect the mutual aid fees from the rickshaw pullers, and promoted the current effective and perfect method of collecting money. However, I feel that I must state here that the Public Concession has no economic responsibility for this association. The method of collecting membership fees from rickshaw pullers is that the rickshaw owners first pay 1.5 yuan per month per rickshaw on behalf of the rickshaw pullers, and the Public Concession then allows the rickshaw owners to collect an additional seven cents of foreign currency from the rickshaw pullers every day. The rickshaw owners pay the money directly to the bank selected by this association, not to the Public Concession. However, when the Public Concession issues licenses to the rickshaw owners every month, the rickshaw owners must first present the bank receipt for the mutual aid fee that has been paid before they are allowed to issue it. At the same time, the Public Concession also has a kind of power of safekeeping and supervision over the finances of the mutual aid association. According to the articles of association of this association, the safekeeping committee members of this association must be appointed by the Public Concession. All expenses of this association must be approved by the safekeeping committee members before they can be paid. Later, the Public Concession recommended three current members of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee to serve as the first three safekeeping committee members of this association. The first duty of the safekeeping committee members is to invite people from the society who are enthusiastic about this kind of welfare work to organize a board of directors. We have already succeeded in this matter, but this is mostly thanks to the participation of enthusiastic people, and in the past six months, they have actively assisted in the establishment of this association. In my capacity as chairman, I would like to thank them." (The rest omitted)

Headquarters Facilities 175

The headquarters of the Mutual Aid Association is located on the second floor of the small vegetable market on Dong Jiaxing Road. The top is triangular and occupies a large area. Most of the buildings are used as dormitories for rickshaw pullers, with three large rooms, each equipped with double iron beds, mattresses, sheets, and quilts. The rest are divided into classrooms, auditoriums, clinics, bathrooms, recreation rooms, conference rooms, meeting rooms, offices, doctor's rooms, infant bathrooms, baby bathrooms, laundry rooms, washrooms, and storage rooms. The facilities are perfect, and it is stipulated that the lodging fee for rickshaw pullers is 60 cents of silver per month, 20 cents of silver per week, and 10 copper coins per day.

Sharp Drop in Silver-Dollar Exchange Rate at the End of the Lunar Year 176

The exchange rate of silver dollars to copper coins in this port was once over 3,300 wen per dollar last year, and silver dimes also reached around 12 dimes and 400 wen. Later, after a period of decline, it fell to 3,000 wen at the Customs, and then gradually increased until February 2nd of this month, when each silver dollar could be exchanged for 3,125 copper coins, and silver dimes could be exchanged for 12 dimes and 256 wen (calculated according to the market rate). Unexpectedly, the next day (i.e., Lunar New Year's Eve), at around 10:00 AM, various tobacco and exchange shops received a report from the foreign exchange house stating that the market rate was 250,000 wen for every 100 yuan, so the retail exchange rate was 2,500 wen per dollar and 12.1 dimes and 100 wen per silver dime. For a time, various tobacco and exchange shops hung small exchange rate signs, with rates ranging from 2,450 wen to 2,700 wen per dollar and 12 dimes and 30-40 wen per silver dime. Double dimes were only exchanged for 400 wen. For a time, the market was so chaotic that the livelihood of the common people was unbearable.

Acclaim from All Walks of Life for the Double-Deck Ferry Terminal 177

The dedicated double-deck steel pontoon built by the Municipal Ferry Management Office of the Shanghai Municipal Government's Xingye Trust Company at the Bund on Beijing Road has been well-received by passengers since it was put into use on the 28th of last month. Moreover, because the number of passengers increased particularly during the Lunar New Year holiday, the terminal's well-equipped facilities and orderly management made it feel less crowded. For days on end, the number of people from all walks of life who came to visit during the holidays was endless. The office provided uniform reception and sent staff to guide and explain in detail. All visitors expressed satisfaction. It is reported that the terminal is the only building of its kind at sea, with a novel and sturdy structure, exquisite and magnificent equipment, and clean and tidy facilities. Furthermore, it faces the Huangpu River and is adjacent to the park on the left, with a quiet and secluded scenery and fresh air, which adds to its appeal. It is truly worth a visit for leisure during the holidays and convenience for suburban excursions.

Yesterday, an order was issued to the Transportation, Mechanical, and Police Departments

The Two-Way Railway Administration issued an instruction to the Transportation Department, Mechanical Department, and Police Department yesterday, stating: "Every year during the winter vacation, a large number of laborers in Shanghai often take the railway train back to their hometowns. During this winter vacation, the Transportation Department temporarily allocated vehicles and added special third- and fourth-class trains every night on the routes with particularly heavy passenger traffic between Shanghai and the towns, and dispatched personnel in advance to explain all the measures to the laborers in major factories. Italian Sculptor Sues Socialite Tang Ying 179

Obtained Tang's Photo Five Years Ago for Promotion

Recently Demanded 3,000 Yuan in Construction Costs, Sued in Court

Mrs. Li Zufa, Ms. Tang Ying, is the sister of Tang Yunlu, the secretary of Song Ziwen, the current standing committee member of the National Economic Commission, who was assassinated at the North Railway Station when he followed Song from Beijing to Shanghai in the past. She is known for her social skills, talent, and beauty, and has been praised as a social butterfly. Five years ago, when Ms. Tang's name was well-known, a sculptor named Shang Qi, an Italian who came to Shanghai from Europe, was still unknown and unremarkable after staying in Shanghai for a long time. No one cared about him, and his door was deserted. Moreover, the cost of living at sea was high, and his pockets were gradually depleted. He felt that it was not easy to live in Chang'an and sighed that he could not return home. Just when he felt trapped, he suddenly heard of Tang's name and thought that if he could obtain this beauty's patronage, he would be able to win the support of all sectors of society. Then, his art would be perfected by the person, and his profits would be guaranteed. Therefore, he obtained a photo of Ms. Tang through various channels, sculpted an image with plaster as the material, and there was no difference between the likeness and the real person. However, this sculpture was not initiated by Tang herself, so after giving the photo, she never asked about it and even forgot about it. Recently, the Italian suddenly sent a letter to Ms. Tang, informing her of the likeness and demanding a construction fee of 3,000 yuan. Tang believed that the original photo was given at the request of a certain person, which was difficult to refuse. Now, after several years, he has made an unexpected extravagant request, so she ignored it. The Italian then hired a lawyer to submit a complaint to the civil mediation office of the First Special District Court, requesting that Tang Ying be summoned to court for mediation. It is alleged that he has been in China for many years and specializes in sculpting stone statues. Five years ago, Tang entrusted him to sculpt a statue with her photo. At that time, because Tang and her husband, Li Zufa, were both well-known figures in society, there would be no problem with the construction cost, so he did not make an agreement immediately and started working. After the statue was completed, he notified her and repeatedly sent letters urging her to pay the price and pick up the statue, but she ignored him. The construction of this statue took several months, and the materials consumed were enormous. The mental energy expended was also immeasurable. Now, even if Tang does not pick up the statue, she should still pay the remuneration and material costs totaling 3,000 yuan. Therefore, he specifically applied for mediation in accordance with the law, requesting that she be ordered to pay. A mediation hearing was recently opened by Judge Zhao Guangju, and Tang Ying also hired lawyer Yang Ruinian to represent her. She stated the reason for giving the photo, saying that Shang Qi used Tang's beautiful appearance to sculpt a statue as an exhibit in order to increase its artistic value and develop his sculpting business. He first asked Tang for a photo as a model, not Tang asking him to sculpt according to the photo. If this work was indeed requested by Tang, why did she not pay the price or pick up the statue for several years, and how could Gao Qi be willing to allow Tang to delay for so long? Judge Zhao then questioned Gao Qi and found that the statements of the two parties were greatly contradictory and could not be reconciled through words. He then announced that the mediation was unsuccessful. Therefore, Gao Qi has now taken a further step and will formally file a lawsuit against Tang Ying.

The Gu Liancheng Futures Cotton and Wheat Case Judgement 192

Gu Ordered to Compensate Losses of Over 14,500 Yuan

Contract Specifies Delivery of Actual Goods, Not Fictitious Trading

Gu Liancheng, a wealthy merchant from Nanxun, signed three futures cotton and wheat contracts with the American company, Meisheng & Co., in September of last year. The contracts stipulated that if the market price decreased before the due date and the buyer failed to pay the margin and sell, the account could be closed at any time, and the buyer would be liable for the losses in full. By mid-November, the company claimed that the prices of cotton and wheat had both fallen, and Gu had failed to pay the margin. Therefore, they closed the account, resulting in a loss of over 14,900 yuan, and filed a lawsuit against Gu for compensation. The First Special District Court summoned the parties and ordered the plaintiff to submit the bills for further review, as reported previously. Recently, Judge Shen Hong held another hearing. The plaintiff's lawyer presented the American

Cotton and Wheat Market Price 193

telegram from November 17, a newspaper published in Chicago containing wheat prices, a letter from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank regarding the US dollar to national currency exchange rate, and the articles of association of the American Exchange. They claimed that the plaintiff, acting as a broker of the American Exchange, accepted Gu's commission to place orders, and all procedures were carried out according to the exchange's regulations. The contract clearly stated the intention to deliver actual goods, and it was by no means fictitious trading. The defendant's defense was untenable, they said. The defendant's lawyer, Yang Linzhi, stated that the bills and other documents submitted by the plaintiff were not official market price reports from the New York Stock Exchange and were difficult to believe. However, this was merely a factual dispute, not the

Main Defense 194

The most important reason the defendant requested the dismissal of the plaintiff's entire lawsuit was that the contract was purely a gambling act. All three contracts stipulated that the buyer should first pay a margin before the seller could place an order on their behalf. If the margin was not paid in advance, there was no obligation to place an order, and the contract could not be considered valid. Since the defendant had not paid the margin stipulated in any of the contracts, the contract was clearly not established, and the plaintiff had no obligation to place an order on their behalf. Moreover, the contract contained gambling characteristics and resembled exchange activities, such as the

Cotton Contract of September 4 195

The delivery date was the end of March, more than half a year away, which did not comply with the exchange's regulations that futures contracts should not exceed six months. The lawyer then cited precedents from the former Dali Court and the Supreme Court regarding fictitious trading and gambling speculation, as well as Article 4 of China's Exchange Law, which prohibits foreigners from establishing exchanges or acting as brokers. He requested that all three contracts be declared invalid. Finally, he solemnly stated that China's economic development was hindered by foreign merchants relying on unequal treaties to engage in economic aggression. For example, foreign-owned banks were not subject to China's

Legal Restraints 196

This prevented the government from implementing a unified economic policy. Now, in addition to banks, exchanges were being established, enticing national dignitaries to speculate and gamble abroad, which was truly heartbreaking. Therefore, although the amount in dispute in this case was very small, it had a huge impact on the future and should be carefully considered, and the contracts should be declared invalid, he concluded. The plaintiff's lawyer, Feisi, immediately refuted this, stating that the case did not involve foreigners operating an exchange in China, but rather Chinese people commissioning foreigners to place orders abroad, which had nothing to do with China's Exchange Law. Transactions of this nature were common, and free trade was not subject to any restrictions. If the transaction in this case was deemed illegal, it would be

Too Far-Fetched 197

The various precedents cited by the defendant were also inconsistent with the facts of the case. In short, the contract contained a "genuine intention to deliver goods," a clear stipulation that proved it was not fictitious trading and did not involve gambling speculation. Because the defendant's attitude was malicious, the plaintiff, in order to prepare for defense, requested that when the judgment was announced in favor of the plaintiff, immediate execution should be declared to avoid difficulties in future execution, he said. The defendant's lawyer immediately opposed the application for immediate execution, adding that

There Was Once a British Merchant 198

Who had a dispute with the Gold Exchange in the British office in this port. The British official ruled that he did not recognize China's Exchange Law. Now, the plaintiff, acting as a broker of the American Exchange, was involved in a lawsuit in our court, and we could also invoke the precedent of not recognizing the American Exchange Law. The plaintiff's lawyer continued to argue for a long time. As a result, Judge Shen declared the debate closed and adjourned for deliberation. At 2 p.m. yesterday, the date for the judgment was announced, and the lawyers representing both sides were present. Judge Shen then ascended the bench and announced the judgment, ordering the defendant to compensate the plaintiff for the loss of 14,508 yuan and to bear the litigation costs. The

Reasons for the Judgement 199

were then summarized and announced, stating that the ordering contract signed by the two parties clearly stated that there was an intention to deliver actual goods upon maturity, which was clearly not fictitious trading. However, because the delivery period was long, the plaintiff stipulated in the contract that the margin should be increased to provide protection and avoid losses in the event of a price decline before maturity. This could not be hastily regarded as fictitious trading. Meisheng & Co. was commissioned by Gu Liancheng to place orders in the United States, so Meisheng acted as Gu's agent. Moreover, the

Goods Transaction 200

took place in the United States, so China's Exchange Law did not apply. Therefore, the loss claimed by the plaintiff was proven by the plaintiff's submission of accounts and should be deemed valid. The defendant, Gu Liancheng, should be held liable for compensation according to the contract. As for the plaintiff's request for the defendant to pay interest of over 400 yuan, the court, after investigation, considered it inappropriate and rejected this part of the request.

The Dredging Bureau Ordered a Large Dredger from Germany to Come to Shanghai 201

Scheduled to Depart from Danzig, Germany on the 8th

The Dredging of the Shentan Project Can Begin Immediately

Datong News Agency reported that the world's largest dredger ordered by the Shanghai Dredging Bureau from Germany has been completed and is scheduled to depart from Germany on the 8th of this month to Shanghai. A Datong News Agency reporter learned that the dredger was ordered for dredging the Shentan outside the Wusongkou, which is closely related to the entry and exit of ships in this port. Yesterday, he interviewed Dr. Chatri, the chief engineer of the bureau, in detail and recorded the details below.

Sailing to China on the 8th 202

The large dredger was built by the German Schiar Shipbuilding Company. The Schiar Shipbuilding Company is the most famous shipbuilding company in Germany, with a machine factory in Elblng and a shipyard in Danzig. After the machine parts of the dredger were completed in Elblng last year, they were transported to Danzig to assemble the hull, which has now been completed. The bureau has also received a notice from the shipbuilding company that it is scheduled to depart from Danzig on the 8th of this month to Shanghai. The estimated journey will take about two months. At that time, Siemens, the agent for the ship, will deliver the goods.

Capacity and Speed 203

The ship was designed by Dr. Chatri, the chief engineer of the Dredging Bureau. The entire ship is 360 feet long and 60 feet wide. The speed is 11 miles per hour when sailing. The speed is only 2-3 miles per hour when fully loaded with mud. The draft is 11 feet when empty and 18 feet when fully loaded with mud. The amount of mud dredged per hour is 3,000 tons according to the contract. The cost is calculated in British pounds, but converted into Chinese currency, it is about 2.5 million yuan.

Dredging the Shentan 204

The sole purpose of the Dredging Bureau ordering this large dredger is to dredge the Shentan outside the Wusongkou. The Shentan is located in the center of the Yangtze River estuary (about 20 miles from the mouth of the Yangtze River and has a large area). The depth is only 17 feet at low tide, so the Jianghai ships entering and exiting the Wusongkou are obstructed. Even Jianglun ships with shallow drafts cannot pass until high tide.

Completion in Five Years 205

After years of research by the chief engineer, it was determined that most of the Shentan was made of mud and could be dredged. Therefore, after the large dredger arrives in Shanghai, the depth at low tide will first be dredged from 17 feet to 26 feet, and the width will be 1,000 feet. The above dredging project is scheduled to be completed within five years, and dredging will continue to be carried out to achieve the plan of dredging a width of 20 miles. The mud dug up will be placed on a beach two miles away from the Shentan.

Wu Tingsheng Went to Japan to Investigate the Manufacture and Transportation of Cigarette Paper 206

Guowen News Agency reported that the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance, in order to address the loss of national tax revenue due to private cigarette manufacturing in various places, had submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance and jointly established the Cigarette Smuggling Assistance Committee with Shanghai Chinese cigarette manufacturers. Since its establishment, the committee has sent personnel to various places to investigate private cigarette manufacturing organizations and the lives of hand-rolled cigarette smokers. It has also found that the cigarette paper sold by British and American merchants is indeed Japanese. Because Japanese merchants do not sell openly, they are distributed by British and American merchants, and the price of the paper has increased accordingly. Chinese merchants cannot bear the pressure, so the committee has come forward to purchase directly from Japanese merchants. Recently, in order to fully understand the manufacturing and transportation of Japanese cigarette paper, the committee specially sent its advisor, Wu Chengtingsheng, to Japan for investigation to learn from their experience.

Giving Out Rice Vouchers at the Qiyuan Buddhist Association 207

The Qiyuan Buddhist Association on Annakin Road in the French Concession has been holding winter relief activities for many years, with the association and Xuan raising funds to set up a porridge kitchen at the Yongxitang address in Xieqiao to provide relief to the common people. This year, it continues to follow the old example and provide relief as usual. Since its opening, the number of people receiving porridge has been increasing daily, reaching more than 10,000. There is less porridge than people, and those who arrive later are given half a catty of white rice. About 20-odd dan of rice are burned every day to make porridge and distribute rice. Because the location is narrow and there are too many common people, it is not enough to accommodate them, and there are fears of danger. On the 23rd day of the twelfth lunar month, the number of people suddenly increased greatly, and the crowds were extremely crowded. The association, fearing the difficulty of management and the lack of funds, had to temporarily suspend operations and discuss better solutions. Later, the great philanthropist He Zhongxiao suggested that the association should continue to distribute rice vouchers at the end of the year, as in previous years, to help the common people get through the year. It was decided to distribute rice vouchers as usual on the 27th day of the twelfth lunar month. More than 8,000 people, large and small, received the vouchers. The association sent many staff to take care of the different sections, and the order was very orderly. The director of the factory, Yu Yuanjue, and Ping Liantang have been consulting with various Xuan and philanthropists to discuss the continuation of the spring relief porridge distribution method, which is still scheduled to be open as usual, which is a blessing for the common people of Hunan in Shanghai. However, the association's financial resources are weak, and the cost of distributing porridge is extremely high. It is hoped that the wealthy gentlemen in Shanghai will generously donate and work together for this good cause. The merit will be immeasurable.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Strictly Prohibits Gambling 208

The Municipal Public Security Bureau believes that the general public tends to indulge in gambling during the Lunar New Year due to habit. As a result, gamblers take the opportunity to profit and cause harm. Therefore, yesterday, it issued instructions to all sub-bureaus and police stations to strictly prohibit gambling. The document stated, "Gambling is the greatest harm to the local area. Ruin, dissipation of time, and unemployment all stem from this. The adverse effects lead to bandits and affect public security. However, every Lunar New Year, the folk custom of crazy gambling has not changed. It should be strictly prohibited to reverse this decline. In addition to the separate order, all must comply and promptly issue a notice prohibiting gambling. This order."

Lawsuit for Counterfeiting Xingxing Brand Coffee and Tea Trademark 209

Sentenced to Imprisonment and Fines

The Gan Tai Candy Company on Megao Bao Road in the French Concession, the Ri Xin Coffee Company in Nanshi, Yu Huanzhang, Yang Jiyou, and others used the names "Yixing Jinxing" and "Xingxing" for coffee and tea, falsely claiming to be the Xingxing brand coffee and tea produced by the Guangzhou Company of Dongxinqiao, and selling them in the market. On the 29th of last month, the case was transferred to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court, and Judge Sun Penghang still presided over the hearing. The police filed a public prosecution through lawyer Fei Xizhen. The judgment was announced on the morning of the 6th, and the defendant Yang Jiyou was sentenced to three months in prison and fined 200 yuan for forging the Xingxing coffee and tea trademark with the intention of deceiving others. The "Yixing Jinxing" and fake Xingxing signs and printing plates were confiscated. The Gan Tai Candy Company was fined 300 yuan for knowingly selling counterfeit Xingxing brand coffee and tea, falsely claiming to be produced by the Guangzhou Company. If dissatisfied, they may appeal. The plaintiff, represented by lawyer Xu Qinfu, requested compensation for losses of 3,000 yuan, and the case was transferred to the civil court.

Agricultural Products Lag Behind, Imports Exceed Exports, Except for Horticultural Products, Which Have a Large Export Surplus 210

The Total Export Value Reaches 19,104,26 Guanliang

However, Transportation and Packaging Methods are Defective and Must be Improved

China is an agricultural country, with farmers accounting for about 80% of the population. The cultivated area is 1,248,781,000 mu. However, the agricultural products produced are not enough for consumption. According to customs statistics, the amount of rice, wheat, flour, etc. imported each year is extremely large. However, vegetables and horticultural products have a large export surplus, with the total export value reaching more than 19.1 million Guanliang each year. This is very gratifying. A Zhonglian News Agency reporter found out the customs statistics as follows. It is reported that from 1927 to May 1931, the average value of imported oranges, fresh fruits, pepper, apples, raisins, agar, other fresh fruits, and confectionery materials, fragrant mushrooms, betel nuts, star anise, longan, lemons, asparagus, dried tangerine peel, lychees, other unlisted fruits, vegetables, spices, nuts, etc. was 9,770,052 Haiguan taels. The total export value of vegetable seeds, walnut kernels, dried walnuts, fresh salted vegetables, almonds, fresh fruits, garlic, melon seeds, oranges, unlisted dried fruits, confectionery, fragrant mushrooms, daylily, canned vegetables, red cabbage, potatoes, fruits, and other horticultural products was 19,104,261 Haiguan taels. In China's foreign trade, imports exceed exports in every category. Now, the export of vegetables and horticultural products actually exceeds imports, which is a great thing to celebrate. However, backward production technology, defective transportation and packaging methods, and inaccurate grading methods all pose a risk of existing products being rejected in foreign markets. It is hoped that domestic horticulturists will pay special attention.

This morning, several Chinese newspapers published reports that the India Mercalli Bank was about to liquidate. This statement is completely false. Record of the First Preparatory Meeting of the Municipal Sports Promotion Association 231

The Shanghai Municipal Sports Promotion Association held its first preparatory meeting a few days ago. The attending committee members included Yu Ziyu, Ding Shoutang, Wang Keyong, Yuan Zengyu, Xiang Xianggao, Shao Rugan, Chen Songchun, Du Yufei, Ma Chonggan, Jiang Huaishu, Qu Yue, Sun Rubin, Lu Lihua, Li Dachao, Chen Yuze, and Hu Zongfan. Shao Rugan served as chairman, and Ding Shoutang as the recorder. The discussion items were: (1) Adoption of the association's first method for soliciting members; (2) Election of Shao Rugan, Wang Keyong, and Ma Chonggan as standing members of the preparatory committee to preside over all proceedings; (3) The association should establish four sections: documentation, accounting, registration, and general affairs, with two staff members in each section, selected from the preparatory committee members by the standing members. The method for soliciting members is appended below:

Shanghai Municipal Sports Promotion Association's First Method for Soliciting Members (1) All initiators of this association are solicitors of members; (2) The members of this association are divided into the following two categories: 1. Individual members; 2. Group members; (3) Individuals with one of the following circumstances shall not be individual members of this association: 1. Those who have been deprived of civil rights and have not yet been restored; 2. Those who are legally incapacitated; 3. Those of immoral character; 4. Those with bad habits; 5. Those who have been proven to have infectious diseases by medical examination; (4) Groups and schools that have not been permitted for record and registration by their respective competent authorities shall not be group members of this association; (5) The representative of each group member of this association shall be one to two persons per group, provided that those with one of the circumstances in Article 3 shall not be representatives of group members; (6) When joining the association, members shall fill out a membership application form, which shall be reviewed and approved by the preparatory committee of this association. The membership fee and annual fee shall be collected by the preparatory office of this association; (7) The time for the first solicitation of members of this association is from now until February 20; (8) This method shall be implemented after being passed by the meeting of the preparatory committee of this association.

Chinese Police Football Team Returns to Shanghai in Triumph 234

Defeated Jinghua in Beijing with a score of 4-1

The Chinese Police Football Team of the Public Concession Police Department, in response to the invitation of the Capital Jinghua Football Team, set off for Beijing on December 29 of the old calendar, with a group of sixteen people led by Inspector Wu Genyuan. They competed at the Lizhi Society Field at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the old calendar New Year's Day. After ninety minutes of fierce fighting, the Chinese Police finally defeated Jinghua with a score of 4-1. There were more than 5,000 spectators, including many important figures from the National Government. It was truly a grand event in the capital's football scene. It is now learned that the team returned to Shanghai in triumph a few days ago (the 5th). The line-up of the team led by Wu Genyuan and Secretary Lu Dagong in Beijing is as follows:

Yin Xingsheng, Ma Bingzhang, Wu Xiquan, Zhu Guijin, Miao Huaguo, Zhang Ziquan, Qian Zuzi, Liao Zhonggan, Dong Zhaobin, Qiu Tiansheng, Yao Jia Gui

Educational News

Chinese Modern Painting Exhibition Scheduled to Open in England 235

丨Starting February 11丨

The Embassy Hosts Two Tea Parties to Entertain Various Circles

Ambassador Guo Explains the Characteristics of Chinese Painting

Central News Agency, London Dispatch: Our country's artist, Liu Haisu, was dispatched by the government to Berlin two years ago to organize a Chinese art exhibition, which won much praise. Many European countries urged Mr. Liu to conduct a traveling exhibition, which successively took place in more than ten major cities such as Hamburg, Rhine, The Hague in the Netherlands, Amsterdam, Geneva in Switzerland, Berna, Prague, etc. Guo Taiqi, our country's ambassador to England, believed that the works collected by Mr. Liu this time were sufficient to represent the modern schools of painting in our country. Therefore, in March of last year, he telegraphed Mr. Liu to exhibit in England, and because London is a large city with a large population, and there are many oriental scholars, the promotion of our country's culture is of utmost importance. Later, because Mr. Liu had prior agreements with authorities in various countries, Mr. Liu did not arrive in England from Geneva until November of last year. After Mr. Liu arrived in England, he immediately designated New Burlington Gallery as the venue and visited artists and art critics, Courtauld Institute of Art of the University of London. Professor Constable, the director of the UniversitvofLondonCourtauldInstiluteofAct, highly respected Mr. Liu's work and provided him with various assistance. On December 12 of last year, Ambassador Guo invited Professor Yan You, Professor P. Yotts, Professor Adaws, Sir Donison Ross, and twelve others from the British University Committee to hold a preparatory meeting at the Chinese Embassy. It was decided that (1) the opening ceremony would be held on February 22, and the press and literary circles would be invited to visit on the 21st; (2) the Crown Prince would be invited to perform the unveiling ceremony; (3) the representative works would be displayed in the museum; on December 29, the diplomatic corps, literary celebrities, the press, and the academic community would be invited for evaluation; (4) Lord Halifax, the Minister of Education, would be invited to serve as the chairman, and Sir Wcllihne Denrlly, Countess Gasford, Sir James Lockhart, Professor Laurence Binyon, and Professor W.G. Conslable, etc. About twenty people were appointed as members. On December 29, Chinese Ambassador Guo Taiqi hosted a tea party at the Chinese Embassy to preview the Chinese paintings for various circles. More than 200 people attended, including ambassadors and ministers from various countries stationed in England, celebrities from the literary and press circles. Many were elderly, and some were middle-aged, all of whom were extremely enthusiastic and fond of Chinese art and very happy to attend the meeting and praise the famous Chinese paintings. Among the modern British literary and art critics, Laurence Binyon, who is insightful and has achieved the highest level of completion in the artistic field, is the most notable. He has written many books and is also the greatest poet. Regarding the criticism of Chinese painting, he has thoroughly published the philosophical thoughts and Chinese people's outlook on life in his book PaintinginheForEas t, as well as the typical historical figures. He also exceptionally appreciated Mr. Liu's works. Ambassador Guo has always enthusiastically supported the exhibition and has written a preface clarifying Chinese painting, saying that Eastern art is represented by China, Japan's culture is imported from China, and the historical timeline of its fine arts is only one-third of China's. Therefore, its paintings mostly echo the colors of China, but lack the charm of Chinese painting. Although India is an ancient civilized country, Buddhism has declined since the Tang Dynasty, and art has gradually declined as well. Therefore, to understand Eastern art, China should be taken as the representative. People in this country have realized this and have launched large-scale exhibitions to showcase ancient Chinese art and modern famous paintings separately. Now, the Chinese Modern Famous Painting Exhibition will open at the New Burlington Gallery on February 21. The main points are briefly described below:

The famous works collected this time were entrusted by the Chinese government to President Cai Yuanpei, Minister Ye Gongchuo, and Professor Liu Haisu, and are all masterpieces of ambassadors from various schools of painting in various parts of China, and Mr. Liu himself also has dozens of his own masterpieces. These works have been exhibited in Berlin, Hamburg, Dusseldorfer, Munich, The Hague, Amsterdam, Geneva, Berne, Paris, and other cities since January 1934 and have received good reviews.

Chinese painting not only focuses on depicting form, but also pays more attention to the expression of the soul. The painting schools mostly regard ink painting as superior, and the painting methods mostly focus on charm and vitality. The first item of the Six Principles is charm and vitality, which is indeed Xie He's insightful view. Art historians and critics of all dynasties have followed it. Although the interpretation of charm and vitality may not be the same in all schools, I will now give a most easily understood explanation, that is, the so-called "qi" refers to spirit, aura, flavor, and interest, that is, the author's own personality and feelings. The so-called "yun" is rhythm, the inner depth of taste. "Sheng" refers to the vitality of life. "Dong" refers to the spirit of movement, which is vivid and prominent. The Ming Dynasty painter Dong Qichang said, "Charm cannot be learned, it is naturally endowed. Read thousands of books and travel thousands of miles to barely learn it." What is the difference between a painting without charm and a camera? The charm of Chinese painting cannot be concealed and naturally appears on the surface of the brush and ink unintentionally. Realistic products of the photographic school have no charm at all and are not only mechanical functions but are also entirely at the mercy of nature, taking the eye as a lens and the heart as a darkroom. Works of art that focus solely on reality are dry and tasteless, so what is the difference between them and a camera? Therefore, Chinese painters are mostly literati who can write and compose poetry, only then can they become masters. From the cultivation of books and poetry flows out purity and uniqueness, flowing out the wonderful taste of intention reaching beyond the brush. Su Dongpo of the Song Dynasty said, "When he puts down his brush, the wind and rain are swift, and the spirit has swallowed what the brush has not reached," that is what it means. Furthermore, in China, not only can painters write and compose poetry, but also the famous politicians of all dynasties can write poetry, paint, and write calligraphy, and some great painters are also politicians, such as Wang Wei and Li Sixun of the Tang Dynasty, Su Dongpo of the Song Dynasty, Zhao Ziyang of the Yuan Dynasty, and Gai Qichang of the Ming Dynasty, are the most prominent examples. "The so-called 'poetry in painting and painting in poetry'" means that poetry, literature, and painting are closely related. This tradition has continued to this day, and this is also a unique phenomenon in Chinese culture.

I am now holding a festival in this country and promoting Chinese culture is my duty. I will briefly describe the special points of Chinese painting as an introduction for the audience. As for what the exhibits are like, it is still up to the experts to evaluate. Guo Taiqi, Ambassador Plenipotentiary to England.

Ministry of Education Issues Order to Study the Case of Shortening School Holidays 236

The case of shortening school holidays and shortening the school year proposed by President Sun of the Legislative Yuan, etc., was previously submitted by the Executive Yuan to the Ministry of Education for review and reply. The Ministry of Education considered that the matter concerned changes to the school year, semester, and holiday dates and should be studied in detail by major educational conferences, education departments, and educational research groups. On the 5th of this month, the original attachment was copied and issued to all universities and educational research groups for compliance, and they were ordered to report the research results as soon as possible for approval.

Ministry of Education Issues Comparative Table of Social Education Funding 237

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating that the statistics of the social education funding amounts reported by various provinces and cities for the 23rd year have been completed. It is calculated that the following eight regions have reached the standard amount: Jiangsu, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Guangxi, Fujian, Henan, Nanjing, Weihaiwei, and the three provinces of Shaanxi, Hubei, and Suiyuan, and Qingdao City. Although they have not yet reached the standard, they are all above 9%, not far from the standard amount. It is expected that they will reach the standard in a short period of time. In terms of the funding amount, Jiangxi Province increased by more than 200,000 yuan, Hubei and Guangxi provinces each increased by more than 100,000 yuan, and Shaanxi, Shanxi, Henan, and Hunan provinces each increased by more than 30,000 yuan. The educational administrative agencies in the respective provinces and cities have made efforts in fundraising and are commendable. As for the percentages of other provinces, some are close to the standard, and some are far away. They should all effectively increase their funding in the next year to meet the needs. In addition to compiling and printing a table and a sequence table of the above reporting materials and issuing them separately, 20 copies of the table and the sequence table of social education funding for the 23rd year of each province and city are enclosed for reference. Furthermore, the number of social education funding for the 21st and 22nd years of the counties and cities under the jurisdiction of the provinces has also been compiled into a table and a sequence table for reference. A total of 20 copies are also enclosed for joint verification. This order.

The relevant departments are currently drafting methods and issuing orders to the provinces and cities for compliance. The remaining cases are not without merit and should be approved for reference by the Ministry. Please be informed, and this approval shall be kept on file."

Wang Zhihua, 4. Lu Pinqin, 5. Ge Liting; 2. Improvement of Minli Girls' Middle School 249

In order to thoroughly improve school affairs, the Minli Girls' Middle School in this city has made some changes to its faculty and staff. Xing Huimin has been re-appointed as secretary, Gu Yanbin as director of academic affairs, Lai Zhiwen as director of student affairs, and Fan Mingyao as director of general affairs. Yesterday, a tea party was held for all faculty and staff to discuss the improvement of the school. Dozens of faculty and staff members attended. First, Principal Tong Hangbai reported on the improvement policy, stating that a tutor system would be strictly implemented in the future, dividing the entire school into fifteen districts according to grade, with tutors being fully responsible for guidance. Staff from the academic affairs and student affairs departments, as well as tutors, will organize teaching and guidance meetings to discuss various plans for progress, integrating teaching and guidance. Other teachers will also adopt a consistent approach with the tutors, hoping to achieve cooperation and mutual assistance. New regulations (divided into two chapters: guidance outline and life norms) will be formulated as standards for guidance. In terms of academic affairs, in addition to reviewing teaching materials and vigorously promoting student study movements to guide their independent research methods, teachers will also observe each other's classes to learn from each other's strengths and make up for weaknesses, in order to enhance teaching effectiveness. In terms of general affairs, scientific methods will be used to train school workers. It is heard that six or seven hundred new and old students have arrived at the school, and registration will close on Saturday.

Central National Physical Education College Recruiting Transfer Students for Grade One 250

Mr. Zhang Zhijiang, in view of the deepening foreign troubles and the imminent danger to the country, which are caused by the neglect of physical education, suggested to the central government two years ago to establish the Central National Martial Arts Hall Physical Education College (referred to as National Physical Education College) in Nanjing, which emphasizes martial arts, physical education, and military affairs, in order to fulfill the responsibility of popularizing national physical education and restoring our country's inherent martial arts. The establishment has only been over a year, and the achievements are remarkable. Students mostly regard entering the college as an honor, and countless people usually come to inquire about the continuation of the examination or request to transfer. Recently, it has been heard that the college authorities, in response to requests from various parties, have specifically decided to hold an examination at the college on February 11 to admit ten male transfer students for Grade One, in order to broaden the scope of training.

Financial Silver Price Rises, Exchange Market Hardens 252

Gold Market Closed, Lacks Maintenance

Very Difficult to Boost the Half-Day Situation

Yesterday's Exchange Market Opened with Spring Festival Holidays, Overseas Calls Came Thick and Fast. London Big Bars Rose by 1.25 for Both Near and Far Term, American Silver Rose by 3.75 for Long Term, and the Silver Market in Montreaux Also Rose by 3.9% to 5.1%. London Pure Gold Shrunk by 2.5 Pence, British to American Rose by 1.125, American to British Rose by 1.25, British to French Rose by 16 Pounds, and American to French Remained Unchanged. The Exchange Market Opened in the Morning with Recent Selling Prices: British Exchange Rate at 1 Shilling 5 and 3125/10000 Pence, American Exchange Rate at 35.1875 Yuan. The Situation After Opening Was Mediocre, and the Central Bank's Listing Was Revealed: British Flat and American Rose by 0.0625, Customs Gold Unit Down by 3 Cents. After That, the Potential Trend Loosened, Because Chinese Merchants Lacked the Appetite to Buy. The HSBC Bank's Listing Was Revealed: British Flat and American Rose by 0.0625, Lacking Transactions. The Silver Balancing Tax Was Revealed and Not Changed, Still Levied at 5.75%. British Exchange Rate Is Calculated at 1 Shilling 5 and 6875/10000 Pence. At This Time, Only Banks Are Doing Swaps. After Entering, Banks' Appetite Varies. However, the Situation Is Still Hard. Reuters Also Had News Correcting the Rumors About the Reform of the Monetary System That Were Circulating Last Week. American Dong and Others Seemed to Be Releasing, Making the Process More Relaxed. By Noon, the Recent Selling Price Was Collected: British Exchange Rate at 1 Shilling 5 and 4375/10000 Pence, American Exchange Rate at 35.5 Yuan. Chinese Merchants Were Not Energetic Because the Gold Market Was Closed, Only the Dalian Gang and Yifeng Yong Were Slightly Buying. Now, the Half-Day Transactions Are Recorded Below:
