A Review of the Cotton Market in the Year 23 of Spun Yarn Flowers 253

Highest and Lowest Transaction Prices and Delivery Quantities of Zheng Biao

Arrival and Sales Volumes of Raw Cotton and Their Monthly Highest and Lowest Prices

The state of cotton in the 23rd year presented a rather active atmosphere in January. It advanced from a low peak towards a high peak. Upon investigating the reasons for its rise, it was said that the United States would forcibly control cotton production, and Penhaide also proposed a plan to limit cotton fields, with the output not exceeding 10 million bales. All kinds of news favored buyers. The meeting on the issue of the Japanese-Indian cotton industry reached a compromise. Indian cotton first tended to rise. On January 3rd, Broach cotton rose directly from 186 rupees to 215 rupees 25. American cotton rose from 1.045 cents to 1.175 cents. The world cotton industry unanimously rose, arousing the activities of speculators. Buyers gathered, and the atmosphere was once heated. Standard cotton rose from over 39 yuan to the highest price of 45 yuan and 10 cents for the May term on February 9th (per picul, based on the Sima scale). By the middle of March, April, and May, unexpectedly, a large tree attracted the wind, and high prices attracted distant customers. Inland sources were crowded, and arrivals increased. Hankou yellow-grade cotton was sold enthusiastically. Unfortunately, the spring sales of cotton yarn were disappointing again. The price of yarn was bleak, and manufacturers felt particularly difficult to operate. Shanghai's stock of yarn was substantial, and the market price was difficult to consolidate, and an unprecedented new low price of 163 yuan was discovered, forming an inverse proportion with the price of cotton. As a result, the cotton market, which was closely related, was constrained. At this time, the American and Indian cotton markets also rose, turning flat after the high. Yarn factories were becoming increasingly concerned about reducing working hours due to the high price of cotton and the low price of yarn. Indian cotton prices weakened further due to the strike of more than 20 yarn factories in Mumbai. Broach cotton fell back to 185 rupees on May 3rd. The low peak of standard cotton for the April term was 40 yuan and 65 cents. By mid-June, coarse yarn sales in North China suddenly became smooth. After the cotton price fell, factories needed to develop, and Shanghai's cotton stocks gradually became thin. Mr. Wang of Tongji Company, in view of the era of old cotton, and with the American and Indian cotton markets and the yarn market moving upwards, organized a very large bullish company. The rumor of short squeezing sang loudly, greatly exciting the weak and sluggish cotton market. The price increase of standard cotton intensified, and Japanese merchants were also in a bullish position. The highest price of standard cotton for the June term was 47 yuan and 55 cents, higher than the similar Indian cotton by 5 to 6 yuan, fully demonstrating the mighty power of the buyers. It was heard that the bullish company made huge profits. By mid-July, August, and September, since the beginning of summer, drought raged in the central provinces. Ponds and streams dried up, and fields cracked. Floods flooded the Northwest and Southwest. When the cotton trees were developing, they suffered such devastation. In addition, on July 1st, the central government implemented new tax regulations, increasing the import tax on cotton from 3.5 gold units per 100 kilograms to 5.0 gold units. With these two factors, the market's sentiment was激昂, and everyone was bullish. The high peak for the August term was over 38 yuan (per picul, based on the market scale). Subsequently, the US government's first estimate was released on August 8th, reducing the output to 9.195 million bales. However, the Shanghai market was unable to pick up. Because Tongcheng Company and Mr. Huang of a certain yarn factory vigorously threw out 100,000 to 200,000 piculs, firmly bearish on new cotton. Therefore, they sold short when American cotton rose, and the market suffered even greater pressure. The reason was that agricultural products were surprisingly cheap last year, but only the price of cotton was high. Farmers changed their crops, and the acreage must increase. The new cotton for the October term fell twice to 37 yuan and 10 cents, then turned downwards. For a time, people were extremely alarmed. On August 20th, the China Cotton Production Statistics Association reported that the acreage was 44,441,047 mu, an increase of 5,283,601 mu compared with the same period last year. As a result, the sellers' morale was even stronger. Afterwards, in mid-October, the United States implemented a policy of buying silver. The silver market soared, and the price of gold tended to shrink, which was unfavorable to our country's prices. During the period when new cotton entered the market, the pressure from sellers became stronger. Therefore, the market situation was unusually weak, with a long period of sideways movement. The lowest price of standard cotton was 33 yuan and 30 cents on October 7th. However, as prices fell, sources from all sides became scarce. Although the cotton stock in the Northwest was thick, most of the goods were absorbed by the cooperative. Another theory was that farmers were firmly determined to hoard and were unwilling to sell. Therefore, although the environment was bad, arrivals were scarce. On October 18th, the national government increased export taxes and added equalization taxes to prevent the outflow of silver. The price of gold soared, and all prices rose together. Paper money rumors rose repeatedly, and rumors of currency inflation were rampant. The market sentiment was greatly shocked. Tongcheng Company reversed from short to long, and the highest price rose again to over 38 yuan. The sharpness of the rise was rarely seen in the past. The situation in November and December slightly weakened. Because the price of yarn was suppressed by the low price of Japanese yarn, the cotton market wanted to rise but stopped. However, Tongcheng and Tongji companies purchased large quantities to go long, kept them closed. Also, because the Indian cotton harvest was poor and the short squeeze was severe, the price increase intensified. The high peak of standard cotton for the April term was once 38 yuan and 75 cents. Recently, the disease of yarn factories due to the high price of cotton and the low price of yarn has become increasingly serious. Cases of factories closing down because they could not maintain operations were heard from time to time, indicating the decline of the yarn factory industry. Cotton industry statistics The last estimate on November 15th showed that the output increased to 11,172,553 piculs, an increase of 1,398,346 piculs compared with the previous year. However, in reality, the price ratio of foreign cotton was too high, and speculators held on without moving. The price of cotton still maintained its outstanding state. Foreign Cotton During the Suspension Period 254

On the 30th, the American cotton market opened, and the market situation was calm. Traders were waiting for the decision on the gold bar case. Prices rose slightly due to purchases in the local area and New Orleans. There were not many deliveries, and new buyers were also lacking. Spot demand was sluggish. The South had some selling, and the foundation was still firm. The closing was firm, with a calculated increase of 457 points. The British cotton market was outstanding, with a calculated increase of 3, 6, and 8 points. Indian cotton initially weakened due to sales by European exporters, but then recovered due to short covering.

On the 31st, the American cotton market was sluggish, and traders were watching. The opening fell slightly in each month due to unfavorable news from Liverpool and profit-taking by bulls. Afterwards, manufacturers bought at limit prices and shorts covered, and the situation improved slightly. Demand was flat. New Orleans sold. Bulls in the March term took profits. Spot sales were not strong. Factories gradually became active, reportedly due to increased sales of Japanese goods. The Fan Queer cotton survey office stated that the cotton acreage was 32,292,000 mu. The closing was flat, with spot prices unchanged and futures prices rising and falling by 12 points. The British cotton market was firm, with a calculated increase of 12 points. Indian cotton weakened due to increased arrivals and profit-taking by bulls.

On February 1st, the American cotton market opened still strong, but because the settlement of the gold bar case was approaching, people's minds were unsettled. Some foreign bulls on the brokerage side took profits, and local parties sold. Buyers were only those who bought at limit prices among traders. There were not many new transactions. Traders were waiting for the export situation at the Washington meeting. Spot inquiries were only from India (Hester estimated that factory consumption this week was 235,000 bales, and Liverpool's inventory was 311,000 bales. The closing was flat, with a calculated drop of 45 points. The British cotton market was calm. Indian cotton initially weakened due to a large number of bull liquidations, but then recovered due to short covering and purchases by European exporters.

On the 2nd, the American cotton market opened, and market prices were mixed. Subsequently, due to unfavorable news from Liverpool, profit-taking by domestic and foreign bulls, and some old bulls reluctantly reselling, prices gradually fell. Traders and shorts bought slightly at the falling prices. Clients generally closed out both sides. Spot goods improved slightly. India purchased cotton produced in the Southwest region, with a calculated drop of 10 to 12 points. The British cotton market was weak. Indian cotton initially strengthened due to purchases by retail brokers, but then weakened due to sales by operators in the market.

Silk and Tea Domestic and Foreign Raw Silk Market Conditions 259

The Local Silk Market is on Holiday

With the US Gold Bar Bill still undecided and people unsettled, stock prices across the board are trending downwards. The silk market has also been considerably affected, so overseas actual sales dare not buy more, and hoarders are all watching and waiting. The Lyon side is even more unmoved, while in Shanghai, because the majority of export firms have not yet opened, silk shops and silk firms are also on holiday, so the silk market remains quiet. Red Plate trading will depend on tomorrow's (the 5th) market conditions.

Overview of Japanese Silk Production and Sales Statistics 260

In recent years, the conditions in the Chinese silk market have followed Japanese prices as the standard for ups and downs, so Chinese silk merchants are extremely concerned about the Japanese silk situation. The production and sales situation for this term (June 1934 to May 1935) deserves attention due to poor production and increased demand. The following is a special introduction of the entire picture to readers, and the general silk industry should also review it.

Spring and Autumn

— (Shen Shou Ruo)

Snippets 267

Shanghai's various circles have officially designated this year as the Student National Goods Year. I believe it should be changed to the Teacher National Goods Year for it to be more practical.

Because students' words and actions usually follow those of their teachers; if teachers desperately set an example by using national goods and strictly train students to use national goods, the students' minds will naturally be deeply imprinted with the words "national goods" and they will reject foreign goods.

There is a local saying in our area that goes, "Hands don't move twenty-four," I don't know what it means, but judging from the tone, it's a description of people who refuse to work no matter what.

Therefore, I hope that everyone will do their duty this year, roll up their sleeves and work hard, really work hard to save the country, and not live up to this saying.

Casual Writing by the Snow Window 268

— Huo Xueming

It has been raining for a few days, the weather is very warm. I thought that at the end of the lunar year, I would not see the sun again, and there would be no more river ice and snow. But a night of west wind swept away the dry leaves in the yard, the water tank froze into glass, the swimming shadows of the goldfish could no longer be seen, and even the snowflakes in the sky were flying vigorously.

The plum blossoms that were budding yesterday secretly bloomed with such charming red flowers in the wind and snow. I sat alone under the window, quietly searching for poetry material for the end of winter, only hearing the footsteps of several skylarks treading on the snowflakes, hearing the singing of the wind drifting from the wall, and also hearing the faint sound of my own heart beating.

Watching the red petals of the plum blossoms slowly disappear, the space is full of powder-like snowflakes, flying little by little, piling up in clusters, decorating the branches of the plum tree purely white, the whiter the fatter, the fatter the whiter. And the sparrows, unafraid of the cold, jump to the east, jump to the west, shake their necks, lower their heads to peck at the snow, take a bite, and then raise their heads to look around. That posture is truly leisurely, pleasant, and graceful!

Suddenly, a girl from the neighbor's house slipped out from the side door of the thatched cottage. She was wearing short boots and a white wool sweater, and walked lightly on the snow. Her bright black hair was stirred and waved by her bouncing steps. She quietly tiptoed after the sparrows, reaching out her hands as if to catch them. But before she could get close, the little sparrows, as if they had a sixth sense, pecked a piece of snow, flapped their wings and quickly flew up to the plum tree, turning around to chirp at the girl. The child stared at the tree eagerly, wishing she could grow wings. And a plum blossom happened to be pecked down by the sparrow, and in the child's eyes, it was caught by her, and she smiled.

The snow is getting heavier and heavier, and the child is walking in the snow, her whole body covered in a vast expanse of white flowers, only revealing half of her small face, which is red from the cold, with two shiny eyes and black, moist waves of hair covering her forehead. ········· The weather is already spring!

I saw all of this clearly from the gap in the window, but I didn't dare to cough once!

General Reaching Out 269

— Yang Yu Sheng

As a rule, a general's hands should be used to hold a command knife and grab binoculars! Using them to play cards or hug women is already an insult to the general's hands! However, the General Reaching Out specializes in using his hands to ask people for money, and he can't even get thousands or tens of thousands of dollars. Think about how embarrassing this is for a "general"!

You sometimes have to wait at the tram stop for the tram, right? Then you should know the General Reaching Out! Although they can't track Wu Zixu and beg by playing the flute, they rarely go door to door begging. And unlike those who sing "Zheng Banqiao Tanhuang" and pretend to be noble by refusing to accept money with their hands, they honestly and impolitely reach out their hands to ask for money, their demeanor is quite dignified!

Some of the generals are missing hands, some are blind, and some are mute. Although their ranks are different, their "nailing skills" are equally brilliant! As long as they see you dropping a copper coin from a cigarette shop and running towards the tram stop, they are ready to greet you! Holding up half an arm or stumbling around and clinging to you. Of course you find it annoying, but you are waiting for the tram and can't leave the station, so you can only dodge your face left and right to avoid him, and he will flatter you from all directions, saying "May you get rich, sir!" You can't get angry, and the tram never arrives, so the cramped situation forces you to spend a small amount of money to get rid of him. This kind of money-grabbing skill is really tough! If it weren't tough, how could they be called "generals"!

"Nailing skills" sometimes need to be combined with "leg skills." I once had the honor of being escorted by a general from Ba Xian Bridge to West New Bridge, and only then was the "ceremony" completed and he retreated! Although I was flattered and felt uneasy at the time, thinking back now, being able to show off my leg strength in front of the general and give him a "longing sigh" is something to be proud of!

It is said that there are also "slogans" when generals use their "nailing skills." The purpose of the slogans is of course to ask for money. But when he encounters two women, he will shout "Two ladies, give one!" This is a bit outrageous! But the "two ladies" can't be bothered to argue with him, and he keeps shouting slogans from behind, so the copper coins clang to the ground, and the general politely "bows" and retreats!

Warmth 270

— Chen Liang

In our house, there are no radiators, no stoves, not even a basic charcoal basin. It is a very spacious, old house, the doors and windows are not complete. In this harsh winter, the wind sharply penetrates the cloth curtains and the window frame holes where the glass is missing, causing the purple copper lamp with a white shell shade hanging in the middle of the living room to shake. Neighbors and relatives often worry about us. "Your house is too cold, isn't it!"

"Cold? I don't feel it."

"We still feel a little warmth!"

Every night, our whole family gathers in this house. Father brings his only confidant, the water pipe, from the shop, a mouth that always wears a smile hiding under a figure-eight mustache, comes back. Mother always happily reports on the day's events, what things in the vegetable market are expensive or cheap, and how pedestrians at the door fought and how she persuaded them to stop, with great enthusiasm. My younger brother and I arrive home no later than six o'clock. Sometimes we buy some things that our parents like to eat on the way back, and we also wrap some separately with our wives, intending to give it to them in the room at night.

We sit around a table for dinner, chat, read newspapers, talk about social news, everyone's mouths, eyes, and noses move in different ways. Sometimes, even our eyes laugh. We forget about this cold season, and we don't know the severity of the north wind.

What fills our spacious, old house is丨

The love of parents, the love of brothers, the love of husband and wife, so passionate!

"We are not cold, on the contrary, we still feel a little warmth."

Little Western Paradise 271

— Written by Zhang Henshui

He had this little idea, and he didn't want to gloss over it. He slept in the room for a while, sat for a while, quietly thinking about how he could borrow Cheng Zhiqian's power to find a good position that wouldn't get him beaten. He pondered for a long time and finally came up with a solution. Maybe the high-ranking director is at the banquet today. I'll write a note on the spot and have the tea boy give it to Cheng Zhiqian, asking him to introduce me to him. He received such a heavy gift from me today, he wouldn't be embarrassed to ignore this little request. In this year when everyone is looking for a job, you have to squeeze forward whenever there is an opportunity, there's no room for careful consideration. He thought about the solution and waited quietly for the time to come. At six o'clock that afternoon, the sky wasn't very dark yet. In the large dining room in front, the two gasoline lamps were still lit at the same time. The whooshing sound of the flames could be heard clearly in the back yard corridor. In this world without electric lights, looking at the bright light through the windows, one could imagine how extravagant the situation was over there. Gradually, the sound of men and women laughing came through the windows. Presumably, the people attending the banquet had already arrived. Zhang Jiefu, with his hands behind his back, paced back and forth in the corridor, looking at the yellowish kerosene lamp light in Cheng Zhiqian's room, which was still on. Presumably, he hadn't gone to the banquet yet. Of course, he had to wait for him to leave before he could talk about what he wanted. He paced back and forth several times, but Cheng Zhiqian was still reading under the kerosene lamp. Even though someone was pacing back and forth outside the window, he didn't even look up. Jiefu wanted to greet him, but then he thought that it was none of his business whether others attended the banquet or not, so why bother with that, so he gave up and went to take a look outside the back yard. Outside this yard was a large open yard, which was where long-distance cars parked for guests from afar. (127)

A Fragrant Record of the Imperial Court 272

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

As soon as the Empress Dowager mentioned this matter, she immediately changed to a very indignant attitude, and her tone was not as gentle as before. "But how do we know! Her appearance is also very upright and beautiful!" Who would have thought that her personality was so clumsy! She treats us as enemies and has never had the slightest goodwill towards us!"

According to the situation of ordinary families, mothers-in-law and daughters-in-law are often the most difficult to reconcile opposing forces in the family, and the reasons are always very complicated and difficult to study. Just like the discord between Empress Dowager Cixi and Empress Jiashun, it has almost long been a public fact, but the reasons for the discord are varied and inconclusive. What I know is that Jiashun fundamentally looked down on Cixi. Why did she look down on her husband's mother? In fact, before entering the palace, she had already known the secret that Cixi had been in love with Ronglu when she was young, so she couldn't help but feel contempt. Especially after Emperor Xianfeng ascended to heaven, the Empress Dowager immediately promoted Ronglu's official position丨In fact, although the Empress Dowager promoted Ronglu, they still could not get close, and even the opportunity to shake hands could be said to be absolutely non-existent.丨Even more dissatisfied Jiashun in her heart; she believed that a woman who was the mother of the world should never have any feelings for another man other than her husband. Therefore, the Empress Dowager, in her mind, was seen as a person who was not worthy of respect! Analysis of Watching 273

— (Xiaoting)

A child who has been away from his parents for a long time, suddenly sees his mom and dad come back, it's like Columbus discovering the New World, there is an unspeakable joy.

A patriotic youth sees the foreign goods displayed in the windows of big stores, it's like a sewing secretary stabbing his hand with a sewing needle, there is an unspeakable pain.

For erotic young men and women, when they meet in the arena of love, the first step is you look at me, I look at you. They explain the principles of looking very clearly.

Ordinary people see corrupt officials, it's like a lamb sees a hungry tiger, deeply afraid of not escaping in time. Corrupt officials see ordinary people, it's like a hunter encounters wild deer and rabbits in the mountains, deeply afraid of not being able to capture them.

Random Talk

The New Year in the Old Capital 274

— Shi Xia

Although the government authorities have repeatedly ordered the people to celebrate the Gregorian New Year, the Chinese people in this place prefer to celebrate the indigenous Lunar New Year, even if the "Lunar Calendar" is called the "Waste Calendar," it's useless. Most citizens are happy to make use of waste. This situation is especially noticeable during the New Year festivals. The Gregorian New Year holidays are only three days for institutions and schools, and have no real relationship with the actual life of the general public. But when the Lunar New Year arrives, the situation is very different, especially in this quaint Beijing, the atmosphere of the New Year festival is overflowing everywhere, whether it is on wide streets or narrow alleyways.

If you are full of "steamed buns" and have nothing serious to do, and you feel that the stove is making your throat dry at home, then a way to pass the time without spending money is to stroll around. If you stroll to Beijing's most lively places, such as Dong'an Market, Xidan Market, Qianmen Street, Dashilar, etc., then you can encounter crowds of people. The social composition of the crowds is also bizarre and complex. There are concubines with eyebrows painted like new moons, noble young ladies with lipstick smeared like fresh blood, retired officials wearing gold-rimmed glasses and leather hats, college students wearing blue cloth gowns, female students wearing men's trousers, old-fashioned ladies with pancake-like buns and feet bound into awl shapes, young masters wearing thick-soled shoes and red capes, simple merchants, coolies in short clothes,········· a variety of characters, it's truly a grand exhibition of people. Some are buying "New Year's goods," some are "joining in the fun." The chaotic shouts of vendors and the sounds of bargaining form an urban symphony. Shops are always piled high with goods, labeled with "big discounts" and "selling out at a loss," tempting their customers.

The so-called New Year's goods are nothing more than "mixed sweets" made of honey dates, peanuts, persimmon cakes, green plums, etc., paper lanterns, rabbit-god lanterns with long fur, stove-king palaces for sending off the stove king, long incense sticks, red candles, melon seeds, watermelon seeds, peanuts, candied fruits, persimmons, etc. These things don't cost much, and most families, big and small, buy them to cook soup, worship ancestors, offer to gods, and fool children, to get through the once-a-year New Year festival. Although the global recession and the turbulence of the North China political situation have made them suffer, the merchants and vendors are not willing to easily let go of the "peak season" of the New Year festival, and they still have to force themselves to cheer up and make arrangements. But those of us who are strolling around can see it very clearly with a cold eye. Although the people in the market are squeezed so tightly, the wealthy old men who are "carelessly" buying goods are ultimately a minority. Most people are just there to join in the fun with a happy mood.

"The scene of the New Year festival in the old capital is lively, but the hearts of most people celebrating the New Year are full of suffering." I thought silently in my heart as I left the market and walked into the dust-filled alley.

Free Talk

Artistic Generalization 275

— Meng Jia

Regarding "Artistic Generalization," Qi Jun's article "Realistic and Romantic" also touched upon it slightly; however, in that piece, the author only discussed it in general terms and did not treat it as a central issue of realistic creative methods.

The so-called "generalization" is not only a special term in art; in science, "generalization" also plays a significant role. However, because the methods of expression are different, the results of their generalization also differ. Here, "generalization" is a key opportunity for realistic understanding. The author extracts the essential, typical aspects from many characters or events and presents them in a comprehensive manner. The so-called "emphasis on characteristics" refers to this.

Generally speaking, the difference between science and art lies mainly in the different methods of expression, that is, the former relies on abstract concepts for realistic understanding, while the latter relies on concrete images. The method of science is to proceed from the abstract to the concrete, while the method of art is to proceed from the concrete to the abstract. However, this distinction is not absolute. The method of science proceeds from the abstract to the concrete, but science cannot exist without the concrete and the intuitive. The method of art starts from the concrete (intuition), but this does not mean that the abstract method of science cannot be applied at all in art. Science is constructed by abstracting and generalizing the diversity and individuality of reality, while art depicts the diversity and individuality in reality as they are. This is generally correct, but not absolutely so, because art also often generalizes reality. For example, when a writer describes characters, he does not describe them one by one, but rather discards the accidental, non-essential differences in many characters and extracts the typical, characteristic aspects (such as habits, interests, desires, beliefs, grammar, etc.) to synthesize into a typical character.

Then, what is the difference between artistic generalization and theoretical generalization? It is often thought that scientific (theoretical) generalization is abstract, while artistic generalization is concrete. This view is incorrect. Because whether it is scientific truth or artistic truth, it is only a manifestation of the objective truth existing in reality, and truth is always concrete. Therefore, the difference between artistic generalization and theoretical generalization does not lie in the abstractness or concreteness of the truth they express, nor in the content of the truth, but in the difference in the forms of expression. Scientific truth is concrete not because it exists in reality as it is, but because it conforms to the essence of reality. However, this alone does not make it an artistic truth. Artistic truth must reproduce the essence of reality in a direct form existing in reality. Artistic generalization also takes not losing the directness of reality as a prerequisite. In this regard, the so-called sensory imagery becomes an issue.

Art, like science, has the task of understanding real life. Therefore, in order to concentrate the power of understanding, it is necessary to cleanse all accidental and non-essential phenomena from reality and further excavate the essence of reality. Here, artistic generalization is the same as scientific generalization, its purpose is to excavate the essence of real life, that is, it is treated as a key opportunity and a method for realistic understanding. Therefore, the correctness or truthfulness of artistic generalization is not only determined by the nature of the writer's point of view, but also by the adequacy of the writer's expression and ability. It is not as simple as Qi Jun said, a matter of "the writer's creative imagination or fantasy." Even if artistic generalization sometimes becomes a brilliant "prophecy" that foresees the archetype of a future era, this is not determined by the writer's rich imagination or fantasy, as Qi Jun said, but by the depth of the writer's understanding of reality, because if a writer wants to understand the future development form of historical laws, he must first deeply understand the past and present development forms of historical laws; after all, the former is nothing more than a higher form of development of the latter.

Regarding the role of generalization in art, the Russian critic Belinsky once said the following incisive words:

"The landscape created by a talented artist on canvas is more beautiful than all the picturesque views in nature. Why? Because there is nothing accidental left in it, all parts are subordinate to the whole, everything tends to one purpose, everything forms a beautiful whole, and so do individual things.

Reality itself is beautiful. But its beauty lies in its essence, its elements, its content, not in its form. In this sense, reality is like pure gold in a lump of ore and earth that has not yet been cleansed. Science and art are like washing away this real gold nugget and giving it a beautiful form."

Therefore, great art is never a non-differentiated record of real phenomena, but should be reorganized and unified from a correct and progressive point of view for reproduction.

Artistic generalization is conditional. And this condition is determined by the object of generalization. When a writer applies the method of artistic generalization, he must pay attention to whether the difference between the two or more phenomena being generalized is essential or accidental. The so-called artistic generalization refers to the difference of the latter. Artistic generalization cannot transcend the era (such as referring to the generalization of era events), nor can it transcend the class (such as the typical generalization of characters). Writers can never generalize events from different eras, nor can they generalize real people from different classes and different lives.

The archetype of a character is concrete and presents different faces depending on the era. "In the 1880s (Russia), intellectuals were disappointed and dissatisfied with the destruction of the revolutionary movement on the one hand, and felt the pain of the slow development of capitalism on the other. In such a rapidly changing era, intellectuals wanted to find their place and happiness, so most of them fell into the dream of the 'small events' theory, only seeking to obtain their own personal happiness, managing the trivial matters of their own personal lives, or running under the banner of Tolstoy's theory, resisting the development of civilization, and only paying attention to the cultivation and completion of private morality." However, with the arrival of the 1890s, with the forward development of capitalism, and the change in the social status of the entire civilian intellectual class, those "unthinking, unemotional" intellectuals who felt that "the colorful clothes of life have faded, leaving only some dull mottled marks," and hoped to find some "happy illusions" in the grave in the 1880s, gradually reduced their misanthropic thoughts and decadence and emotions, and in their souls, burned the joy of life and the longing for a bright future. The typical characters in Chekhov's works in the 1890s are mostly those who "look ahead boldly with their heads held high." Nadezhda, who abandoned her hometown and ran to Moscow to study in "The Betrothed," is also presented as a representative of the new symbol. The emptiness of the past has disappeared in the lives of the new characters. What is burning in their hearts now is the bright future 丨 the longing for civilian freedom.

In a word: Artistic generalization is conditional; therefore, the image of the so-called typical character should also be era-based and class-based. In this sense, great works that excavate the essence of a specific stage of history should also be epoch-making labors.

— Zang Kejia

You ask me,

How tight are the days before the New Year?

You better ask yourself.

Ask the people in the cities and the countryside.

ⅩⅩ

One red strip after another seals

The doors of store after store,

"Closed for business" is a long poem of blood and tears,

Endless sorrow for you to ponder.

ⅩⅩ

Hope struggles in everyone's footsteps,

After a thousand turns, it finally falls to the ground!

In the countryside, the owner of the thatched house flees from debt,

The dog hugs the debt collector's pole more fiercely than a tiger.

The woman's single trousers become lanterns in the wind,

Helplessly running east and west,

"Human feelings are as thin as autumn clouds" is not an empty saying,

The color of money is most revealing at this time.

ⅩⅩ

Seeking life in death, people step onto dangerous paths,

A kitchen knife turns an honest man into a robber.

No one is guarding the year-end,

But how many lives cannot get past this hurdle!

Bodhi Temple 277

— Xiangshan

Longing for the Bodhi Temple, where lonely flowers bloom.

Living outside the city, from the time the sun hangs on the beam of the temple well, I sneak into the cemetery behind the temple. In this aisle of lonely graves, with the heart of a monk or nun, I wander back and forth.

There are no monks in the temple, only an old man watching the temple, languidly holding a broom, leisurely sweeping the white plum blossoms pecked apart by chickens.

The loveliness of the Bodhi Temple lies in the cemetery behind the temple. The cemetery has a kind of unrhymed silence, which is a simple and sentimental poem; on the marble or granite tombstones are engraved the names of people who have passed away, which can make people recall the rise and fall of the so-called touching and tragic history. Moreover, the moss-covered mouths of the tombstones can make people feel the sorrow of the wilderness.

When alive, they are all strangers, but after closing their eyes, strangers gather in this small cemetery, equally covered with fallen plum blossoms, equally listening to the sound of the temple keeper striking the bell, without joy, let alone jealousy, all quietly comforted in the winter sunshine.

In front of the tombstones are placed stone basins, carved with stone, the clear water reflects the clouds of the sky, when the cold wind howls down from the withered branches, passing over the water surface, the ripples of small lines, fold the clouds. And the shadow of the grass flower inserted in the water basin, also trembling slightly, the water droplets condensed on the grass flower, like beads, fall into the basin, whether these water droplets are the tears of the mourner, who knows? These water droplets are crystal clear!

On the roof ridge of the main hall of the Bodhi Temple, there are countless sparrows, basking in the winter sun, the noisy sound, breaks the afternoon silence of the cemetery. If the sound of the shotgun rings out in the distance outside the temple, the sparrows will fly in the clear sky like black sesame seeds, and when the sound of flapping wings disappears, the cemetery will appear even more desolate and monotonous; making myself, wandering in the aisle, feel a terrifying stillness; mistaking the warm sun for the cool moon.

Last winter, when I was avoiding the cold in Ito Onsen Township on the Izu Peninsula, I stayed in a boarding house near a certain Bodhi Temple. Ito is a water town, the front window faces the clear blue sea, and the back window is the cemetery behind the Bodhi Temple. Behind the cemetery is the gradually steep, withered yellow winter mountain. At dusk, the fog-like night falls from the sea, and the steam from the hot springs in the back mountain gradually sinks to the foot of the mountain, crossing the cemetery and hanging on the back window; at this time, I indulge in meditation alone, sitting cross-legged, and I feel a kind of grey shadow in my heart, drilling in from the back window, feeling a kind of sharp and chilling pleasure.

The temple keeper in this temple is a suave old man. Whenever the night is late, there is often a kind of intense, desolate, and sad sound coming from the old man's room. This is the old man's only pleasure, the sound of the "shakuhachi"! The "shakuhachi" can often emit sounds of resentment, sorrow, and grief, like the Qiang flute outside the Great Wall, which can evoke homesickness, but sometimes I am often fascinated by this sound, and I can't help but shed tears. These tears are warm. Let me make a rash analogy! This mood of tears is like the mood of a guilty child repenting in the arms of a loving mother.

Often when I wake up in a dream, I hear the mournful sound of birds in the cemetery under the back window: when I can't stand it, I put on my clothes and open the "rain door" of the back window, and the ground is full of bright moon, clear and sharp like a white blade dancing in front of my eyes, the tombstones are dyed crystal white, only the dense shade of the main hall falls on the frost, black and white contrast, there is a kind of indescribable interest; and the plum trees in the foothills, like white mist, low on the ground, the fragrance of yellow and the faint smell of the sea, make me feel a special taste. And thus the longing for the Bodhi Temple is even deeper.

Whether it is a flower or a bell in the temple, it contains the magic power to make people feel emotional and meditate. Especially in the corner of the temple, or under the trees, the stone statue of Jizo, standing alone, can make people forget their pain. The Jizo statue is a smiling, slightly fat ascetic, his body is covered with the traces of wind and rain erosion, but the smile on his face still smiles at everyone; wearing a red alms hair and a cape, with traces of crow droppings on his body, but still smiling plainly, in the human world, I am afraid that only this stone statue of Jizo can find such a smiling face!

Looking at this Jizo, I can recall the classic dance recitation drama "Otsuya Kyoran," how Otsuya, an abandoned woman, goes crazy in front of the Jizo statue, and the Jizo still smiles without saying a word. Why can't the stone Jizo give Otsuya passion and comfort? Is this smile a sneer? It made me shudder.

Now I live in a remote alley far away from the Bodhi Temple. Every day, I am tired of the noise of the city and the sound of machines. When I sit silently by the window or in my dreams, I often feel that I am still wandering in the cemetery of the Bodhi Temple, looking at the tombstones, water basins, wells, and smiling Jizo, and especially silently reciting the fact that the stone slab once left my footprints, and that I have wandered back and forth hundreds of times in the aisle, and when I am in pain in my heart, it is a soothing and peaceful good medicine. I am longing for the Bodhi Temple. The Bodhi Temple still often blooms with lonely flowers, and in the early spring, it is still overflowing with an air that is more mellow than wine.

The Bodhi Temple is desolate, and the cemetery behind the temple is even more desolate, the lonely graves stand silently under the trees.

The Celebrated Jumping Frog (1) 278

— Mark Twain, translated by Libo

Complying with a friend's request in a letter from the East, I went to visit Simon Wheeler, a gentle, loquacious old man, to inquire about my friend's friend, Leonidas W. Smiley—as my friend requested—the result of which visit I will write below. I have a nagging suspicion that Leonidas W. Smiley is an imaginary person; my friend has never known such a person; he is simply calculating that if I ask old Wheeler about him, it will remind him of that wicked Jim Smiley, and he will start to tell some long, foul stories that are useless to me and make me terribly annoyed. If that was the purpose, it was achieved.

In a dilapidated hotel in the decaying Angel's Camp mining district, I found Simon Wheeler, the old fellow dozing comfortably by the fireplace in the saloon. I noticed that he was fat, bald, and that his placid face bore a charming expression of kindness and simplicity. He jumped up and greeted me with a "Good day." I told him that I had a friend who asked me to inquire about a childhood intimate friend named Leonidas W. Smiley, the Reverend Leonidas W. Smiley, a young missionary, who he had heard had once been a resident of Angel's Camp. I added that I would be very grateful if Mr. Wheeler could tell me anything about the Reverend Smiley.

Simon Wheeler pushed me back into a corner and began the following monotonous story with his chair. He never smiled, he never frowned, he never changed the rounded key from which he had plucked the first word, he never betrayed a single suspicion of emotion; but throughout the entire endless story there ran a poignant ardor and a sincere pulse, plainly showing me that he had not the slightest idea that there was anything strange or ridiculous about his story, that he regarded it as a real and important matter, and that he admired the two protagonists in it as remarkable geniuses in chicanery. I let him go on at his own convenience, never interrupting him once.

"The Reverend Leonidas—why, the Reverend—well, there used to be a fellow here named Jim Smiley, in the winter of '49, or maybe it was the spring of '50—I don't remember exactly, anyway it was one or the other of them two times, because I do recall him coming to the Camp when the creeks hadn't dried up yet—but he was a most curious man, always wanting to bet on anything he saw, the opposite way from other folks, mind you; and if he couldn't find anybody to bet against him, he'd change sides. Anyway that suited him, I reckon—anyway, so long as he could get a bet, he was satisfied. But he was lucky, uncommon lucky; he always come out winner. He was always ready to bet on any opportunities; there warn't any get-at-able thing that he warn't ready to bet on, and I told you he'd as lief bet on one side as t'other. If there was a horse-race, you'd find him either flush or busted at the end of it; if there was a dog-fight, he'd bet on it; if there was a cat-fight, he'd bet on it; if there was a chicken-fight, he'd bet on it; why, if there was two birds settin' on a fence, he would bet you which one would fly first; or if there was a camp-meetin', he would be there regular to bet on Parson Walker, which he judged to be the best exhorter about here, and so a good man. If he see a straddle-bug start to go anywheres, he would bet you how long it would take him to get wherever he was going to, and if you took him up, he would foller that straddle-bug clear to whatever place he was bound for, or clear to Mexico. Lots of the boys here has seen that Smiley, and can tell you about him. However that don't signify—it was just a natural gift. Pahrson Walker's wife laid very sick once, for a good long time, and it seemed as if they warn't going to save her; but one morning he come in, and Smiley asked how she was, and he said she was considerable better—thank the Lord for his infinite mercy—and coming on so smart that, with the blessing of Providence, she'd get well yet; and Smiley, before he thought, says, "Well, I'll risk two-and-a-half that she don't."

Notice to Telegraph Senders 279

1. For the name and address of the recipient within 15 characters, it will be calculated as 5 characters. Beyond this, fees will be calculated by character.

2. Using a telegraph code name to send a telegram can save characters.

3. Using the telephone to send and receive telegrams can save time.

4. If the matter is urgent, you can send an express telegram.

5. To avoid errors, you can send a verification telegram.

6. If you do not want the other party to spend money, you can prepay the reply fee.

7. Where there is no telegraph office, you can send a postal transfer telegram.

8. To check for typos, you can ask the telegraph office to send a free telegram to inquire.

9. If the recipient's whereabouts are uncertain, you can send a follow-up telegram.

10. Where there is a station but no telegraph office, you can send a railway telegram.

11. If several people are in the same place, you can send a distribution telegram.

12. Where there is no post office or telegraph office, you can send a special delivery telegram.

13. For weddings, funerals, greetings, illnesses, promotions, transfers, birthdays, etc., you can send a social telegram.

14. For urgent applications for funds, you can send a telegraphic money order to the post office.

15. When telegraphing abroad, please add (Cgra) to ensure accuracy and reliability.

For details, please inquire at various telegraph offices or radio stations, or write to our company for inquiries. Our company address is No. 769, Zhongshan North Road, Nanjing.

The Voice of the Telecommunications Industry

Sino-Italian Communication Report 281

— Lü Bing

In the past year, the International Radio Station established by the Ministry of Communications has opened direct lines to the United Kingdom and Japan in addition to the original circuits. There has been obvious progress in business, and telecommunications revenue has also increased.

Recently, the Sino-Italian Communication Report was also established. News transmission between Shanghai and Rome can be achieved in an instant through the station. The International Radio Station has been planning a wireless network for communication with the world for years. After a lot of effort, as of now, all important cities in the world have direct circuits that can be connected. Although it cannot be said to be exhaustive, its achievements are also very gratifying to us.

It is found that the sound of Sino-Italian communication has been very loud last year. The preparation period was relatively long. The initial test results were not bad. The perceived shortcomings were that the electrical power of the Rome radio station was slightly weaker, which had an impact on reception. Before opening, we had to be extra cautious, so we technically improved it again and re-tested it. After both parties considered it satisfactory, it was officially opened for business on the 21st of last month. The situation is actually like this.

The initial launch of Sino-Italian communication was not at the request of our country, but at the request of the Italian government. It is slightly different from the situation of communication with other places. The relationship between Italy and our country is closer, and business has developed a lot in recent years. In addition, it is noted that our country's international radio stations have a good reputation for handling overseas communications. Therefore, the Italian side is very eager for Sino-Italian communication, and after consideration by our side, it also expressed sympathy, so it was decided to follow. Now that it has been implemented, the satisfaction of both China and Italy is self-evident.

European countries, such as England, France, Germany, and Russia, have all communicated directly with our country's radio stations one after another. Rome is the political center of Southern Europe, and Shanghai is an important commercial port in our country. There are quite a few expatriates in each other's countries. International trade depends entirely on the intelligence of telecommunications, and in terms of political affairs, Italy has promoted us in precedence, which shows that Sino-Italian relations are becoming more progressive. For the sake of friendship between the two countries and for the sake of our country's international wireless telecommunications business, the Sino-Italian communication report is undeniably important. This is brought up in the hope that our countrymen will pay close attention to it.

On Telephone Arrears 282

— Zhen

In the fourteenth issue of this publication, the author once wrote an article "On Government Telegram Arrears," outlining the general amount of government telegram arrears and the reasons for the arrears. The conclusion was that the economic difficulties of the telecommunications administration were due to the accumulation of government telegram arrears, and the solution lay in strict enforcement. In recent years, the Ministry of Communications has strictly investigated and seized private matters sent through government telegrams, and has also made every effort to collect cash at half price for government telegrams. Except for military telegrams for bandit suppression, which only require the cost of materials, no other telegrams can be sent on credit. This has been repeatedly ordered and followed by the National Government, and government and military agencies have also shown considerable understanding, and people in society have even more sympathy. Therefore, it is not difficult to start the reorganization. However, telephone arrears have not yet been noticed, and the amount owed is huge, reaching 2,500,934 yuan and 89 cents as of June of the 23rd year of the Republic [1934]. Such a figure is quite alarming! The total amount of monthly rental fees owed by users of each telephone bureau is as follows:

Table of Monthly Rental Fees Owed by Users of Each Telephone Bureau
